Japanese Troops Attack Deng's Unit at Fengcheng Without Success

Japanese Troops Suffer Over 100 Casualties

(Beiping) Japanese troops have launched two attacks on Deng Tiemei's unit in Fengcheng, both without success. At the end of last month, the Japanese army dispatched more than 300 soldiers from Jin, along with more than 1,000 members of the puppet Manchukuo Jing'an team, to attack. They engaged in battles for more than ten days at Longwangmiao, Beijingzi, Chenjiabaozi, Yawobao, Baiqibao, Jinjiatun, and other places, all without success. Our various units simultaneously received a letter from the enemy, which read: "To whom it may concern, I, the humble officer, was ordered to suppress you and your unit. Since arriving in Fengcheng, I have heard that your reputation is very great. If you intend to seek blessings for the people and surrender, I will certainly handle it well. I hope you will send a representative to arrange a meeting place and discuss everything. Team leader, Tomita Harunari." Our side ignored it. Later, the two sides made contact again. The Japanese army suffered more than 100 casualties, including one colonel, and retreated towards Fengcheng. Our side suffered more than 20 casualties and captured many spoils of war, including the Japanese army's abandoned Jinzhou gate pass, gold medal, and photos of the attack on Tang Juwu's army. The enemy troops are still distributed around Fengcheng, appearing very frustrated. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Beiping) The Volunteer Army, composed of Deng Tiemei, Liu Jingwen, Li Zirong, Wang Quanyi, and other units, totaling over 10,000 people, is now united. From the Liao River to Longwangmiao in the eighth district of Xiuyan, all areas are occupied by these units. The Japanese are planning to immigrate to northern Manchuria, Jilin, and eastern regions via the Anfeng line in the middle of this month. The Volunteer Army has learned of this plan and intends to sabotage the railway as passive resistance. The Japanese have strengthened their defenses, stationing heavy troops at all stations along the railway line. (Special dispatch, 1st)

Commander Cao Yucheng of the Jilin National Salvation Army Dies a Martyr's Death

Captured by the Traitor Li Shoushan

(Tianjin) According to returning passengers from Changchun, the Jilin National Salvation Army achieved excellent results last year, causing many deaths to the enemy and traitors. Last winter, the enemy and traitors suppressed them with heavy troops, so they retreated into the deep mountains to await an opportunity to rise again. Unexpectedly, the enemy and traitors discovered their location and launched a joint attack by land and air forces. From December 10th, they fought fiercely for three days and nights. Running out of ammunition and without reinforcements, our Cao Yucheng suffered serious injuries and continued to resist, leading to his capture by the traitor Li Shoushan. Li initially intended to persuade him to surrender in order to incorporate his troops. Cao cursed the traitor vehemently and died a martyr's death at Dagushan on the morning of the 17th. Vice Adjutant Feng and follower Zhao Wensheng were also subjected to slow slicing death. Our Jiang Kui regiment was surrounded and had no choice but to be incorporated into the puppet army. The Xu Huchen and Wang Baoxu regiments retreated to the Xiangxu Gully area. The Li Xiangyun and Xia Shenqi regiments retreated to Longzegou. Their ammunition and supplies are all exhausted, placing them in a tragic situation. The army sent a representative, Wei Yuntai, to Tianjin to request assistance. However, he has not been able to find an office to work from, so he went to Ping yesterday to contact the National Salvation Association. There has been no progress yet. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Harbin) The leader of the Righteous Army, General Xi Chao, and his entourage arrived in Jiamusi from Baoqing yesterday. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Japanese Commander Addresses Soldiers

Chinese Police Replaced with Indians

(Hankou) The situation in the Japanese concession has gradually become serious since the military conference. The military attache, Okamura, also declared to the Japanese residents at the same time that the Third Foreign Fleet of the country has a strong presence on the Yangtze River. The ammunition currently available on each ship can sustain continuous firing for eight hours a day for ten days. The Japanese consulate is also collecting anti-Japanese writings from newspapers in Beijing, Shanghai, and Hankou to investigate the responsible parties. The Chinese police in the Japanese police station have been replaced with Indians, and many people have been hired to expel Chinese from the concession. (Special dispatch, 1st)

British Ambassador Arrives in Beijing Yesterday Morning

= Visited Luo Wen-gan Twice to Exchange Views =

= Luo Wen-gan Hosted a Banquet to Welcome Him =

(Nanjing) British Ambassador Sir Miles Lampson, who took leave to return to his country last May, returned to China last month. During his stay in Hong Kong, he inspected places such as Guangzhou, Shantou, and Xiamen and visited the southwestern authorities. He arrived in Shanghai on the 25th of last month, where he stayed for a week, engaging in many social activities. He took the Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Ruihe ship to Beijing on the evening of the 30th. He arrived at Xiaguan at 7:00 AM on the 1st. The British Consul in Beijing, secretaries, counselors, and foreign guests who had friendly relations with Lampson all went to the Jardine Matheson wharf in Xiaguan to welcome him. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs also sent many personnel to welcome him. Lampson shook hands with the welcomers and drove directly to the British Consulate in Sajiawan to rest. Those who arrived in Beijing with Lampson included Chargé d'Affaires O'Gorman, Secretary Black Penn, Counselor Scott Tait, Chinese Secretary Techman, and eight other counselors. Lampson went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in the afternoon to meet Foreign Minister Luo Wen-gan, Vice Minister Xu Mo, and Director of the European and American Affairs Department Liu Shishun. Foreign Minister Luo also scheduled a banquet at the Diplomatic Residence tonight to welcome Lampson and invited the heads of various departments and councils to attend. It is rumored that Lampson's arrival is to facilitate negotiations between China and Japan, but this is not confirmed. He will stay in Beijing for about a week before going to Ping. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) British Ambassador Secretary Scott told a reporter that Lampson came to Beijing from Shanghai on his way back to Ping to have some contact with Foreign Minister Luo and will stay for about a week before returning to Ping. He will come to Beijing again in two months. If the situation in North China becomes urgent, he may move south ahead of schedule. If the Sino-Japanese issue deteriorates, British interests in the Yangtze River area will be affected. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) According to a source, when Lampson met with Foreign Minister Luo Wen-gan, in addition to exchanging greetings, Lampson explained that the attitude of the British representative Simon at the League of Nations meeting on the Sino-Japanese issue was not intentional partiality. Amid the rising tide of small countries unanimously opposing Japan, Britain had to take the position of a major power to mediate the atmosphere of the meeting. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) After arriving in Beijing on the 1st, British Ambassador Sir Miles Lampson visited Foreign Minister Luo Wen-gan at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs twice, in the morning and afternoon, to exchange views in great detail. It is said that Minister Luo expressed that the recent alienation in the feelings between China and Britain due to Britain's attitude in the League of Nations was deeply regretted and hoped that Britain could change its position to a fair one so that the friendly relations between the two countries could be further consolidated. Lampson, who has been in China for many years, has always had a very harmonious relationship with China and especially hopes that this return to China will further promote the relations between the two countries. It is said that Lampson was very moved and promised to make efforts to restore the relations between the two countries. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Central Political Council Resolves to Establish Administrative Regulations Review Committee

= Appoints Dai Chuanxian as Chairman, Sun Ke and Song Ziwen as Vice-Chairmen =

Also Resolved...

Appointed Personnel Engaged in Public Service

Are Regarded as Civil Servants When Subjected to Disciplinary Action

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council held its 342nd meeting at 9:00 AM on the 1st. The following members attended: Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, Sun Ke, Ju Zheng, Chen Guofu, Dai Chuanxian, Zhang Renjie, Wu Jingheng, Lin Sen, Yang Shuzhuang, Chen Gongbo, Shi Qingyang, Ma Chaojun, Liu Shouzhong, Zhou Qigang, Mao Zuquan, Zhang Daofan, Luo Jialun, Zhao Pilian, Gu Zhenggang, Tang Youren, Zeng Kuoqing, Wang Luyi, Chen Shuren, Wang Qi, Zheng Zhannan, Jiao Yitang, Guo Chuntao, and more than 30 other people. Ye Chucang presided over the meeting, and the following resolutions were passed:

1) An Administrative Regulations Review Committee will be established under the Central Political Conference. Dai Chuanxian, Sun Ke, Song Ziwen, Yu Youren, Wu Chaoshu, Ju Zheng, Ye Chucang, Zhu Jiahua, Huang Shaoxiong, Jiao Yitang, and Niu Yongjian were appointed as members. Dai Chuanxian was appointed as the chairman, and Sun Ke and Song Ziwen were appointed as vice-chairmen. 2) The proposal by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to revise the organization of local administrative agencies was referred to the Legal System Group and the Political Report Group for joint review. 3) The proposal to establish Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureaus in various treaty ports was submitted for review.

4) The National Government will issue a decree commending Xing Guangshi from Haimen, the inventor of the spinning machine, and grant him a pension of 10,000 yuan.

5) Appointed personnel engaged in public service shall be regarded as civil servants when subjected to disciplinary action. Those appointed by central government agencies shall be handled by the Central Civil Service Disciplinary Committee, and those appointed by local government agencies shall be handled by the Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee.

6) The Central Executive Committee is requested to elect Zhou Zhenlin and Xu Shaozhen as members of the National Government.

7) The resignations of Deng Jiayan and Chen Bozhuang, members of the Legislative Yuan, were approved. Zhou Wei and Zhao Naichuan were appointed as members of the Legislative Yuan. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of disciplinary action for malpractice by appointed personnel in various agencies, the Control Yuan had submitted a request to the Central Political Council to determine a method. The Central Political Council has now resolved that malpractice by appointed personnel should be regarded as malpractice by civil servants and punished according to the law. (Special dispatch, 1st)

Inauguration of the Third Congress of Beijing Municipality

=Central Government Sends Zhang Ji to Deliver Instructions=

(Nanjing) The Third Congress of the entire Beijing Municipality was inaugurated at the Municipal Party Headquarters at 9:00 AM on the 1st. Present were Central Committee members Zhang Ji, Chu Minyi, Shi Ying, representatives from various Yuan (branches of government), ministries and commissions, and over three hundred representatives from district party headquarters and sub-branches. Lei Zhen, Chairman, reported on the preparations for the Congress and gave a speech, stating that all representatives should take responsibility and work for the Party during this time of national crisis, striving to be a model for the entire country. Afterwards, Zhang Ji, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, delivered instructions, encouraging all party members to practice frugality and work hard to save the country from its crisis. He also described the importance of the He River situation, stating that if the He River were to fall, the Northeast would be difficult to recover, Tianjin and Beijing would be difficult to defend, and the Japanese could advance directly into the country, and so on. Subsequently, Chu Minyi and Shi Ying also gave speeches. At 2:00 PM, five members of the presidium and seven members of the proposal review committee were elected. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM, with the first meeting scheduled for the 2nd. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Chen Gongbo Talks About the Sulfuric Acid Plant, Which Can Be Realized Soon

(Nanjing) Chen Gongbo said that China's sulfuric acid used to be supplied by foreign imports. In order to develop state-owned industry and commerce to prevent the outflow of rights and interests, the Ministry planned to fund a large-scale sulfuric acid plant. However, since the Incident in the Eastern Provinces, all industries have been exhausted, the national treasury's income has decreased sharply, and the national finances are extremely strained. If it were to be run by the government, it would be difficult. Therefore, it was presented to the Central Government for approval to be jointly run by China, Britain, and Germany. China would contribute six million yuan, and Britain and Germany would contribute five million yuan, for a total of eleven million yuan. Of China's six million yuan, three million yuan would be contributed by the business community. The British side has now appointed a plenipotentiary representative, Bolida Dagu, to come to Beijing to discuss with the Ministry. In response to the current needs of industry and commerce, the Ministry plans to contact the British and German parties immediately. After concrete methods are negotiated, it will begin to implement the plan, which should be realized within this year. German New Prime Minister's Negotiations with the Central Party Break Down

Anticipation that Parliament Will Be Dissolved Within Days

A Nationalist Party cable from Berlin on the 1st reports that German Prime Minister Hitler's negotiations with the two Central Parties (i.e., the Catholic Center Party and the Bavarian People's Party) have broken down. It is anticipated that Parliament will definitely be dissolved within a few days. However, whether the date will be before the meeting scheduled for February 7 or after the meeting is still difficult to predict.

A Nationalist Party cable from Berlin on the 1st reports that the German President has signed an order to dissolve Parliament and delivered it to the Cabinet. If necessary, it can be announced at any time. Now that the Cabinet has this order, it has temporarily become a de facto dictatorship. According to afternoon news, the Cabinet will hold a meeting this afternoon to discuss the parliamentary situation, because the Cabinet does not currently have a majority of support in Parliament. However, it is believed that it will not be difficult to achieve this now that the National Socialist Party holds power. It is also reported that the Cabinet will send the order to dissolve Parliament signed by the President to Goering and instruct him to prevent Parliament from meeting, because Goering is the administrative commissioner of Prussia and has control over all Prussian police. The Cabinet's request to dissolve Parliament today was caused by the fact that the Social Democrats were about to submit a motion of no confidence as soon as Parliament opened. If Parliament is dissolved, it is expected that the general election will be scheduled for March 5, and the government can implement its policies during this period without fear of interference from others.

A Nationalist Party cable from Berlin on the 31st reports that after the establishment of the new German government, it has now begun to organize various urgent matters. According to the Berlin Local Instructions, the first step of the new cabinet is to mediate the differences between industry and agriculture, so that both parties can cooperate with the government. In this way, the government can engage in economic plans for prosperity, and unemployed people can be rapidly relieved. The Local Instructions was founded by the new Minister of Economic Affairs, Hugenberg, so the news carried by the newspaper can of course be regarded as the most rapid news from the cabinet. In addition, the cabinet will also discuss how to organize the short-term debts owed to various countries. As for the people, since the establishment of the new cabinet, the negotiations with the Catholic Center Party have reached what point, and whether the party is willing to cooperate with the new government. These issues are of the most interest. Today, the new Prime Minister Hitler had a long talk of more than two hours with leading figures of the Center Party, such as Cass and Frick. It is said that Cass raised many questions to Hitler and asked him to answer them one by one. Whether the Center Party can cooperate depends on the answers. Hitler will submit the discussions to the cabinet meeting tonight. According to newspapers, the government is quite willing for Parliament to agree to continue the meeting for several months, and is also quite willing for Parliament to pass a bill allowing the cabinet to have full power to deal with urgent issues. However, the passage of such a bill must be achieved with the consent of more than two-thirds of Parliament, which is difficult to achieve due to the opposition of the Social Democrats and Communists. Therefore, the new Minister of Interior, Frick, has indicated that the dissolution of Parliament in the future may still be unavoidable. He hopes that the results of the re-election will be more progressive than what it is today.

A Nationalist Party cable from Berlin on the 31st reports that the German capital's stock exchange has announced that the new government will adhere to the legal scope and not make any economic attempts, which has led to the financial sector's concern. Therefore, the market value of all securities has greatly improved today, with price increases ranging from two pounds to seven and a half pounds. Furthermore, the theory of a restored capitalist tendency is quite strong, which is also one of the reasons why the securities market is scrambling to buy.

Main Conference on Disarmament

Discussing the Issue of Revealing Violations of the Convention

A Havas cable from Geneva on the 31st reports that the Presidium of the Disarmament Conference met this morning to discuss the issue of announcing or revealing violations of the future Disarmament Convention. The Presidium still had inconsistent opinions on the issue of protecting those who announce or reveal violations. The Spanish representative, Madariaga, did not think the hesitant attitude was right. He said that the Spanish government supports providing protection to those who reveal violations. The French representative, Massigli, proposed concrete methods for the convenience of discussion, namely: 1. If a country violates the Disarmament Convention, and a private person reveals it, if that person is not an employee of the state, then no criminal responsibility shall be imposed on them. 2. If the person revealing the violation intends to slander, their punishment should also be made public. Otherwise, the international committee should send a member to participate in the debate. 3. If the person revealing the violation is a civil servant, they shall also receive the same protection, provided that they notify the relevant official in charge of the event they wish to reveal in advance. The French representative's suggestion was submitted to a special committee for review. Chairman Henderson declared that the General Committee will meet on Thursday afternoon to discuss the disarmament and security construction plan proposed by France.

Zhang Fakui's Impressions of Traveling in Geneva

=Everything at the Disarmament Conference is Controlled by Powerful Nations=

=At League of Nations Meetings, Military Force is Justice=

Former Commander of the Fourth Army, Zhang Fakui, has been abroad for a long time. When the violent Japanese bombarded Shanhaiguan, it was rumored that Zhang would return to the country to participate in the anti-Japanese effort. Recently, a letter from Zhang, dated December 19th from Paris, was received. It is recorded here to inform those who are concerned about national affairs and interested in Zhang's whereabouts. The letter roughly states: "I arrived in Suez on the morning of November 28th and traveled by car to Cairo to view the pyramids and the Sphinx, and inspected the far-right politics of the Italian Fascist Party. I arrived in Rome that day. This place was the base of Christianity and the old church two thousand years ago, from which they engaged in conquering the world. Moreover, Romans were skilled in architecture and sculpture, so the ancient relics left behind are still ubiquitous today, enough for tourists to browse. Italy completed its national unification in the late 19th century, but education was immature, industry was backward, corruption was rampant, bandits roamed the land, and beggars filled the city. It has long been despised by countries around the world. Since the Fascist Party, led by Mussolini, marched into Rome and took power, they have actively reformed politics, severely punished corruption, revitalized education, developed industry, and eliminated bandits and beggars. It has not been a full decade, and Mussolini's integrity, dedication to the country, and incorruptibility have created Italy's current position. On the evening of the third day, I went to Venice. The city has over a hundred small islands, with over a hundred waterways for boats to travel through, intricately interwoven like a net, and over three hundred bridges for people to walk on. The entire city has no vehicles. Looking from afar, the entire city seems like it is best seen at night. I arrived in Berlin on the thirteenth day. I participated in the Geneva Disarmament Conference. The result of the conference is still a set of empty words. In fact, everything is controlled by the powerful nations. Even the League of Nations is nothing more than the only mechanism for imperialists to divide spoils. Furthermore, at this League of Nations meeting, although there were representatives such as Yan, Guo, and Gu who were skilled at debate, weak countries have no diplomacy, and military force is justice. How could they possibly counter the unreasonable behavior of the Japanese representative Matsuoka? I believe that in this era of the strong preying on the weak, one should understand the lesson that military force is justice and not hope that others will uphold justice. The scenery is extremely beautiful. I originally intended to stay there for many more days, but I cannot tolerate being bullied by Japanese slaves here, nor can I watch the so-called League of Nations uphold justice. Therefore, yesterday, I accompanied Brother Yizhi on a trip to Paris, England, and southern Germany."

Qing Yi's Failed Usurpation

=Xi Qia and Ronghou Plotting Restoration=

=Japanese Side Heavily Angered, Detaining Representatives=

Changchun Correspondence: The Puppet Manchukuo's executive, Puyi, previously had plans to usurp the throne after the abolition of the old calendar, proclaim himself emperor, and advance to become the emperor of the Later Qing Empire. It is now heard that this matter has been discovered by the Japanese side, who ordered it to cease. The representatives of various groups who were elected to go to Changchun to urge Puyi to ascend the throne have mostly fled and dispersed, except for a small number who were arrested and imprisoned by the Japanese military police. It is said that this plot was orchestrated by the puppet Jilin Province Governor Xi Qia, the puppet Central Bank President Ronghou, and Puyi's close associates Bao Xi and Deleng'e, among others. Since Xi Qia became a traitor, he originally intended to use foreign force to succeed in restoring the Qing dynasty, planning to imitate Shi Jingtang's fatherly service to the Khitans. Therefore, when the puppet state was founded, national public opinion vehemently denounced him as a traitor, but Xi remained calm and even said to others, "Who is a traitor and who is not will be clear in the future. My aim is to support the Qing dynasty and succeed in its restoration. Moreover, I am a Manchu Qing royal, so what is wrong with a Manchu Qing royal carrying out a restoration movement? Wait until it becomes clear what kind of person I am; half a year will be enough." This was his ambition, and also the intention behind his willingness to lead wolves into the house. Unexpectedly, for a year now, Xi Qia has felt that his idealized Qing dynasty restoration movement is becoming increasingly distant from success. Even the actions of the deposed emperor and his own political power are subject to the control of others. He then believed that the unsoundness of the puppet state's system might be due to the incorrect designation. If Puyi were to be crowned emperor and obtain Japan's recognition and military assistance, he could also gain a new position internationally. At the same time, Japan's oppression and sanctions would naturally be eased, and the people of Manchuria would also be aroused by old ideas and sincerely submit to the new country. Therefore, he secretly planned everything with Ronghou, Bao Xi, and others, and enlisted several Japanese people within the Puppet Concordia Association, enticing them with high titles and great benefits, and proceeded separately. He secretly sent personnel to Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang to give instructions to various groups, ordering each group to elect two representatives to gather in Changchun for a formal petition, and then submit a memorial urging Puyi to ascend the throne. Once the order was issued, the Japanese side would be notified. At that time, even if the Japanese side were unwilling, they would have no choice. This matter progressed rapidly a month ago, and the representatives from various regions had all arrived in Changchun before January 15th, residing in major hotels. They were planning to hold a meeting at the Yuexiangchun Hotel on January 18th, but the Japanese side detected it. On the 16th, they dispatched military police to various hotels to search for and arrest the representatives who had arrived from various regions. Over ten people were immediately arrested, and the rest fled upon hearing the news. Those who were arrested confessed the truth, and the Japanese side was extremely angry. Muto Nobuyoshi summoned Xi Qia, Ronghou, and others, and scolded them severely, saying that they should not secretly carry out a restoration movement and harbor ulterior motives. He ordered them to be detained for two months. Later, after many people interceded, saying that it would be appropriate to be lenient during this League of Nations meeting, Muto finally agreed to release them. This scene of the restoration movement was thus cut short before it matured. It is heard that Puyi has recently become seriously ill due to excessive indulgence in opium and women. Zheng Xiaoxu does nothing but drink wine and write poetry every day. All political orders come from the hands of the Japanese Chief of the Puppet General Affairs Office. The heads of various puppet departments seek instructions from the Japanese before dawn and dusk. The Japanese Chief of the General Affairs Office then seeks instructions from Muto. The situation is even worse than it was a few months ago. (January 24th)

Xu and He's Remnant Bandits Will Be Annihilated

=Tian Songyao Goes to Sichuan to Supervise the Suppression=

=He Chengjun Returns from Xi'an to Hankou and Then to Jiangxi=

=Hunan and Hubei Armies Coordinate to Encircle and Suppress He Long's Gang=

Hankou Correspondence: Xu Xiangqian and Kuang Jisun's remnant bandits fled to northern Sichuan, where they were severely suppressed by Tian Songyao, Liu Cunhou, and other Sichuan army units, suffering heavy casualties. The bandits are now surrounded on all sides, and it will not be difficult to annihilate them in one fell swoop. Initially, the bandits fled to Hanzhong, intending to invade Gansu, but due to the gathering of national troops, they were unable to succeed. They then fled into Sichuan, hoping to take advantage of the fierce fighting in Sichuan to penetrate deep into the area, recruit gang bandits, replenish their strength, and open up nests in the overlapping mountains, holding onto strategic locations. Before they fled to Tongjiang, the Sichuan war ended. Tian Songyao's Luo Naiqiong, Li Weiruo, and Liu Hanxiong units were all calmly mobilized and coordinated with Liu Cunhou's unit. At the same time, He Chengjun also ordered Hu Zongnan, Liu Maoen, and other divisions to track and suppress them from Shaanxi. The bandits repeatedly counterattacked but were all repelled. Although the bandits still number 20,000, they have only 8,000 rifles. Recently, a portion of them fled to Bazhong, further weakening their strength. Commander-in-Chief Chiang, in order to thoroughly eliminate the bandits, specially appointed Tian Songyao to concurrently serve as the Director of Bandit Suppression in the Sichuan-Shaanxi border area, responsible for clearing them out. Tian took office in Chengdu on January 28th and appointed Sun Zhen, Deputy Commander of the 29th Army, as the front-line commander. Tian and Sun are scheduled to depart for Sichuan on February 1st to supervise the suppression. In addition to the Luo, Li, and Liu units, Dong Zongxiu, Zeng Xiantong, Wang Mingzhang, Huang Zhengui, and other divisions will all be fully mobilized, leaving only one brigade to defend Chengdu. It is heard that Tian will issue orders for a general suppression on all fronts upon arriving in Sichuan. He Chengjun, having completed the arrangements, can temporarily leave Shaanxi. He originally planned to go to Nanjing from Xi'an to meet with Chiang and report on the progress, but learned that Chiang had gone to Jiangxi. He then decided to return to Hankou by plane from Xi'an on February 1st and then proceed to Jiangxi to seek instructions.

When Xu's bandits fled to Sichuan, He's bandits also entered Hubei from Shaanxi. They initially captured Hefeng, then hid in Laifeng, and attacked Sangzhi in western Hunan. These were all places where He's bandits had previously been based. There were not many garrison troops, so they were able to drive straight in. After Sangzhi was captured, the Hunan army made strict defenses. He's bandits once invaded Yongshun but were repelled. Now, coordination between Hunan and Hubei has been established. The Hunan army units of Chen Quzhen and Li Jue are concentrated in the Jinshi, Fengxian, Cili, Dayong, and Yongshun areas, under the command of Li Jue. The Hubei army units of Jiang Zuojun and Zhang Gang are concentrated in Yidu, under the command of Fan Xiji. The encirclement and suppression have now begun. The bandits' strength is even weaker than that of Xu and Kuang. The local people have long been ravaged and hate them to the bone. Therefore, although He's bandits have fled back to their hometown, they have no ability to rally support. The date of their destruction is not far off. The authorities believe that the western and northern parts of Hubei are critical hubs for the fleeing of various bandit gangs. In addition to ordering Xu Yuanquan's unit to be stationed in western Hubei, Xiao Zhichu's division has also been transferred to northern Hubei. Yu Zhaolong's brigade of Xiao's unit arrived in Xinye on the 31st. Wang Jinyong and Chen Yong's two brigades arrived in Zhengzhou and are heading south in batches, with one brigade designated to be stationed in Xiangyang, one in Fancheng, and one in Laohekou. The handover should be completed before February 4th. (January 31st)

Jiangxi Province's Newly Designated Bandit Suppression Year

Party and Government Personnel Focus on Bandit Suppression Work

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi Province has been in a state of red terror for seven years. As of now, of the 81 counties in Jiangxi, the following are completely occupied by bandits: Zixi, Jinxi, Yongxin, Ninggang, Lianhua, Ruijin, Shicheng, Ningdu, Xingguo, Xunwu, Anyuan, Huichang, Guangchang, and Hengfeng. These counties exist in name only. The cities are barely protected, or the bandits come and go when the troops leave, causing endless disturbances. There are 42 counties, including Ji'an, Yongfeng, Ganzhou, Anfu, Guixi, Tonggu, Dexing, etc., where the situation is unsettled and bandits appear from time to time. Only about 20 counties, including Nanchang and Jiujiang, are stable and free from bandits. This time, Chairman Chiang came to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression and dispatched the 80th, 83rd, 88th, 23rd, and 87th divisions to strengthen the military force. All members of the Provincial Party Headquarters and Provincial Government held the second joint meeting yesterday. In order to demonstrate their determination to suppress bandits, they also decided that 1933 would be designated as the Bandit Suppression Year in Jiangxi. The legislation is as follows: 1. The Provincial Party Headquarters and Provincial Government will jointly issue an emergency order, instructing Party Headquarters and government agencies at all levels to concentrate manpower, resources, and time on bandit suppression work as the central task. 2. A declaration will be issued, with Committee Member Li Zhongxiang appointed to draft it. 3. A letter to the people of Jiangxi will be issued, drafted by the Provincial Government Secretariat. 4. A work program for bandit suppression will be determined, including: 1. Propaganda, 2. Comfort, 3. Transportation, 4. Disaster Relief, 5. Blocking of Bandit Areas, 6. Trade, 7. Road Repair, 8. Procurement, 9. Rescue, 10. Investigation. 5. A joint meeting of all sectors will be convened on January 28th. 6. A propaganda outline will be determined. 7. Bandit suppression propaganda will be expanded. In addition, the Post-War Committee established by the Provincial Party Headquarters and Provincial Government will also depart with the army to work at the front, handling post-war reconstruction and disaster relief in the recovered bandit areas, as well as various self-defense matters. (January 25th)

Shandong People Raise Funds to Purchase Aircraft for Air Defense

=The Impression of the January 28th Incident is Deepened=

=All Sectors Donate Funds to Resist Aggression=

Jinan Correspondence: The January 28th Incident of last year inflicted a painful and deep wound on the people of the country. Time flies, and in the blink of an eye, a year has passed. All sectors of Jinan held a memorial meeting for citizen representatives on the 28th at the Provincial Party Headquarters to express mourning. Several hundred representatives from Party and government agencies and various groups attended the meeting, following the usual procedures and bowing three times to the martyrs of the January 28th Incident. Then, Chairman Zhang Zhangcun reported on the purpose of the meeting, followed by Industrial Department Director Wang Fangting, representing the Provincial Government, and Qin Qirong, a member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, discussing the necessity of solidarity and resistance to aggression, and recounting the war history of the 19th Route Army's resistance against Japan in Shanghai and the martyrdom of the car driver Hu Amao, with impassioned words and tearful voices. Finally, five proposals were passed: 1. Issue a telegram to the whole country vowing to resist violent Japan to the death and recover lost territory. 2. Send a telegram to all generals in the country urging them to unite to resist Japan's aggression. 3. Send a telegram to the League of Nations requesting a fair resolution of the Northeast Incident as soon as possible and adopting decisive and effective measures to stop violent Japan's aggression, otherwise the League of Nations should be responsible for the breakdown of peace in East Asia. 4. Send a telegram to the whole country calling on people from all regions to voluntarily donate funds to purchase aircraft and strengthen national defense, aiming to achieve the goal of having one aircraft per county. 5. Organize the Jinan People's National Salvation Fund-Raising Committee. At this point, the chairman did not report organizing the Jinan All Sectors People's National Salvation Aircraft Fund-Raising Committee. The Provincial Party Headquarters has now sent letters to the members, including Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu and all members, various committee members of the Provincial Party Headquarters and County Party Headquarters, Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie, Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kairu, Banking Association President Lu Zhuan, Jinan Chamber of Commerce Xin Zhujiu and Miao Xingcun, various trade associations Zhang Guansan and Fan Chongde, and Wang Zhanyuan and Li Tianni from various sectors, among others, to hold a meeting in the coming days to elect committee members and immediately begin operations. The Shandong Provincial Aircraft Collection Committee has been established for quite some time, and has been very effective. The donations received have already reached 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. Recently, Shen Honglie, Commander of the Bohai Fleet and Mayor of Qingdao, sent a telegram stating that all officers and soldiers of the navy donated 10,000 yuan, and the Qingdao Municipal Government and all its agencies also donated 10,000 yuan, which was remitted by the Bank of Communications. In addition, the Zaozhuang Zhongxing Coal Mining Company donated 20,000 yuan, the Ningyang Coal Mining Company donated 5,000 yuan, and in other areas, businessman Liu Zishan may donate 5,000 yuan, and wealthy gentleman Wang Zhanyuan may donate several thousand yuan. Many people from various agencies and sectors are rising up to respond, so it is not difficult to raise millions of yuan, which can be regarded as optimistic. (January 29th)

Songjiang

Winter Grain Tax Extended for One Month

The deadline for the winter grain tax for the 21st year is traditionally the lunar New Year's Eve. Overdue payments are subject to late payment penalties. However, due to the drop in rice prices last year, the rural economy is in a state of panic. Therefore, on New Year's Eve last year, the collection office saw a significant decline in revenue. The Finance Department has now issued a telegram allowing a one-month extension for the winter grain tax for farmers. Those who pay the winter grain tax within this period will be exempt from late payment penalties to show compassion. The county's First and Second National Tax Collection Offices have now begun collecting taxes.

Finance Bureau Ordered to be Abolished

The Provincial Government, due to the exhaustion of provincial funds, plans to abolish various bureaus under the county and merge them into the county government to establish departments for management in order to save expenses. This will also streamline administrative efficiency. The Finance Bureau has now informed the county magistrate that it must be closed by the end of February and will be jointly managed by the county government starting in March. There have not yet been clear orders regarding the abolition and merger of other construction and education bureaus.

Suzhou

Shengjia Village Tragedy: Appeal Filed with the Supreme Court

The widely publicized Shengjia Village tragedy, in which the main offender, Fang Ziqing, was sentenced to a fine of 600 yuan in the initial trial by the local court, was appealed to the High Court, which acquitted him on January 31st. Now, the victim's family has entrusted attorneys Zhang and Wang to file an appeal with the Supreme Court. The original prosecutor has also declared an appeal.

Robbery and Injury in Hengjing Township

In the Upper Lane Village of Hengjing Township, which borders Taihu Lake, a bandit boat arrived at 8:00 AM on the first day, carrying over ten bandits armed with machine guns. They landed and rampaged through Zhu Fusheng's house, looting to their hearts' content before leaving. As they left, they fired two shots, injuring a long-term worker, Zhou Chunshan. Fortunately, his life is not in danger.

Wuxi

Construction Department Stipulates Width of Third Under-the-Slope Street

The widening of the Third Under-the-Slope Street has been in dispute for several years and has not yet been implemented. Since the organization of the Widening Committee, progress has been actively pursued. It has recently been approved by the Construction Department and will continue to follow the original width classification table set in April of the 20th year, setting the total width, including sidewalks, at 8 meters. It is also permitted to temporarily not construct sidewalks and implement the 6-meter plan. After receiving the order, the Director of the Construction Bureau immediately convened a meeting of the Widening Committee to discuss engineering planning. Based on the above guidelines, an engineering design and budget estimate were drafted and submitted to the county government yesterday for forwarding to the Construction Department for review.

National Goods Exhibition Opens

The National Goods Exhibition, jointly organized by the Shanghai National Goods Traveling Propaganda Group and the local Popular Education Center, has been in preparation for over ten days and is now ready. The opening ceremony was held at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Jiahui Hall in the park. The venue is located at the former site of the park's tennis court, and two pavilions have been erected at the park's entrance and exit to enhance the spectacle, with red and green lights hung along the route. Over forty well-known national goods factories from Wuxi, Suzhou, and Shanghai participated. Staff members have been separately appointed, and a special publication has been published to promote the event.

Changzhou

Inviting Merchants to Operate Long-Distance Buses

The Wu (Jin) Yi (Xing), Wu (Jin) Dan (Yang), and Tong (Jiang Yin) Jiang (Ning) three highways have been built, and the bridges and culverts have also been installed. However, the road surface has not yet been paved. Previously, residents of Wujin, Yu Dajun and others, submitted a request to the provincial departments to open a long-distance bus service on the Wu (Jin) to Dan (Yang) section of the Wu (Jin) Dan (Yang) Road. Now, the provincial government has decided to invite merchants to undertake the bus operation. A fund of 100,000 yuan must first be raised for road repair expenses. Those who contribute funds will receive the exclusive right to operate the buses for ten years. After the expiration of the term, they may apply for an extension. The county government received the instruction yesterday and issued the measures, ordering that merchants be invited immediately to undertake the operation in order to facilitate bus traffic.

Nantong

Details of the Jiangsu Guerrilla Unit's Rebellion

In the spring of the 20th year, the Jiangsu Provincial Security Department recruited the sea bandits under Shen Fengshan, numbering 500 men, and organized them into the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Security Guerrilla Brigade. Over 300 of them were stationed in Lvsi. At around 10:00 PM on the 29th of last month, due to a dispute over pay, they mutinied. Except for 27 men stationed at the City God Temple, the rest went to Lvsi Town, Qintuan, Sanjia Town, and other places to loot, firing guns to demonstrate, killing and injuring Chen Zixi and a Jiang surnamed female servant, among others. Over 500 households in the entire city of Lvsi were looted, with losses reaching over 200,000 yuan. When the mutinous soldiers retreated, they also kidnapped over ten people, taking five boats out to sea. One of the boats sailed to Kenshou, where it was intercepted by the Industrial Special Police Team stationed there. Yue Haining, the company commander of the Second Company, requested to surrender. In addition to Yue, there was also the first platoon leader, the third platoon leader, and a total of thirteen soldiers. They were all disarmed and, at 10:00 AM on the 31st, escorted to the county government for transfer to the Provincial Security Corps Headquarters in Tongcheng. After this incident occurred, the Provincial Security Corps stationed in Nantong and Haimen counties immediately dispatched troops to intercept them and telegraphed the Provincial Security Department for instructions. They were ordered to cooperate with the county magistrate to properly handle the aftermath. Zhu, the commander of the First Regiment stationed in Tongzhou, also telegraphed the county magistrates of Tonghai, Qi, and Chong on the 31st, instructing them to disarm and forward any mutinous soldiers encountered to the regimental headquarters for reporting.

Zhenjiang

Land Value Tax Extended with Added Surcharge

The Zhenjiang County Finance Bureau announced the collection of the second installment of the 21st year's land value tax, which is the originally assessed amount of grain, but the deadline for collection has passed. The collection has already been announced, and staff have been dispatched to urge the collection officials to obtain clearance receipts from the various villages and order the summons and recovery of various outstanding cases. Now that the two-month deadline for collection has passed, a surcharge should be added according to regulations. However, considering the continuous rain and muddy roads, which make travel between the city and the countryside inconvenient, the bureau has requested and received approval from the Finance Department to extend the deadline for one month with added surcharge. It is reported that this has been widely announced and the collection officials have been instructed to immediately go to the various villages and urge the village head and other personnel to collect the overdue taxes from door to door, and within ten days, collect all the outstanding payments for the various installments of the 21st year's land value tax, as well as the outstanding installments for the 20th year's land value tax, and submit the payments to the treasury.

Yangzhou

Opium Case Suspects Escorted to the Province

Regarding the case of over 60,000 yuan worth of opium in the county's seventh district, the provincial government ordered the county government to arrest and escort the public officials involved in the case to the province for interrogation. The county government has already escorted eight people, including the district bureau chief, regimental commander, and patrol officer involved in the case, to the provincial capital on January 30th.

Shaoxing

Commercial Situation After the Great Clearance

Among the various industries in Shaoxing, those that profited the most after the Great Clearance were soy sauce shops, due to the abundant grain harvest last year, low raw material costs, and still high selling prices. The next most profitable were cigarettes, kerosene, hardware, money shops, and foil shops. Other industries were average. Tea, silk cocoons, and silk fabrics were overstocked due to sluggish sales. Huangjiu (yellow wine) was also unable to be shipped out due to the impact of the war. The bamboo products produced in Zhoujiaqiao suffered greatly from sluggish export sales.

Ningbo

Bandits Kidnap Villagers

In Zhuangjiawan, near Huang Gu Lin, Yin County, resident Xu Songlai, who made a living selling firewood, was usually frugal and hardworking. Unexpectedly, at around 10:00 PM the other night, five bandits suddenly came and kidnapped Xu Songlai. His wife, upon seeing this, grabbed onto Songlai and refused to let go and was also beaten severely.

Meningitis Outbreak in Cixi

In the Zhangting area of western Cixi, meningitis suddenly broke out the day before yesterday. The patients are mostly young children, and the infection is spreading rapidly. Several people have died in a single day. Families with children are greatly panicked and are rushing to hospitals to get preventive shots.

Page 13

Local News

Reactions to the Liu Yusheng Execution Case

Regarding the case of Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, executing Liu Yusheng, editor of the Zhenjiang Jiangsheng Daily, the Chinese League for the Protection of Civil Rights and the Shanghai Journalists Association both considered the case to be of great importance and discussed it at their meetings yesterday. As a result, they issued declarations expressing strong opposition. Gu Zhutong will also submit a statement to the Executive Yuan to defend himself. Details are listed as follows:

Declaration of the League for the Protection of Civil Rights

Firmly Protect Civil Rights, the Press Expresses Support

Declaration Outlines Three Demands to the Government

Chinese League for the Protection of Civil Rights

Yesterday, in response to the Liu Yusheng case, the League for the Protection of Civil Rights was in contact with the Shanghai press, exchanging views. The details are described below:

Executive Committee Meeting

Due to the declaration issued regarding the Liu Yusheng case, the Executive Committee held a meeting at approximately 3:00 PM on the 8th floor. Attendees included Madame Sun Yat-sen Soong Ching-ling, Cai Yuanpei, Lin Yutang, Israel Epstein, Chen Binhe, Zou Taofen, and others, totaling ten people. The discussion resulted in the decision to first issue a Chinese and English declaration to the nation and request that the government severely punish Gu Zhutong.

Reception

Subsequently, the League prepared tea and snacks on the 8th floor to receive the Shanghai press. Over forty reporters from various newspapers attended, including Shi Liangcai, General Manager of Shen Bao, who was also present. Chairman Cai Yuanpei first reported on the reason for the reception and read out the declaration. He then invited those present to express their opinions for exchange and reference. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

A GlimPSE OF OPINIONS

(I) Madam Sun Yat-sen, Soong Ching-ling, advocates that the Shanghai press should lead a one-day strike by the national press to show resolve; (II) Cai Yuanpei advocates that the press should issue a declaration regarding the Liu case, requesting the government to severely punish Gu Zhutong in order to uphold the truth and handle the matter according to the law, so that those who violate the law will be severely punished; (III) Shi Liangcai stated that the press regards this matter as particularly personal, and should naturally express itself appropriately. He is willing to be responsible for submitting discussion methods to the Newspaper Association, but his statement is personal and cannot represent any organization. In addition, Lin Yutang, Zheng Zhaofen, Xie Wugang, and others advocated that the national press should unanimously criticize the case in their commentary. Shen Bao reporter Qian Hua advocated requesting party and national elders Madam Soong Ching-ling and Mr. Cai Yuanpei to make strong representations to the government. Finally, Mi Xingru, a reporter from Shen Shi News Agency, gave a detailed report on the Liu case and advocated severely punishing Gu Zhutong, as well as those who were proactively involved.

ISSUING A DECLARATION

The China League for Civil Rights issued a declaration regarding Gu Zhutong's execution of Liu Yusheng, stating that recently, Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, illegally executed Liu Yusheng, the manager of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, and resisted the Supervisory Yuan's investigation beforehand. This bloody case is exactly the same as the atrocities of the Northern Warlords in Beijing who executed Shao Piaoping and Lin Baishui. The people of the whole country should pay serious attention to it. The people should enjoy the absolute right to freedom of speech and publication, which is the right that citizens of modern civilized countries should enjoy. Even if Liu Yusheng had illegal acts beyond the scope of "freedom," he should be handed over to the judicial organs for trial according to the law. The administrative organs must not illegally detain him, let alone illegally execute him. However, Gu Zhutong abused his power, not only illegally detained Liu Yusheng for as long as five months, but also brazenly resisted the investigation by the Supervisory Yuan. After resisting the investigation by the Supervisory Yuan, he further illegally executed Liu Yusheng and sealed up the Jiangsheng Newspaper Office. This dark atrocity of trampling on human rights and destroying laws and disciplines has clearly proved that Gu Zhutong is essentially no different from the Northern Warlords, and is also the public enemy of our national people. In order to safeguard human rights, the people of the whole country should rise up together to make a firm resistance to Gu Zhutong's warlord atrocities. Moreover, such an extremely dark atrocity is not limited to Gu Zhutong's execution of Liu Yusheng alone in our country today. (Omission) This League is organized to safeguard civil rights and fight for civil rights. This League expresses its firm opposition to Gu Zhutong's atrocities of illegally executing Liu Yusheng. At the same time, this League believes that Gu Zhutong, as an incumbent administrative official, openly disregards the law and tramples on civil rights. If the government cannot control such atrocities, it will be a great shame to the government. This League hereby makes three demands to the government: (I) Immediately dismiss Gu Zhutong and other responsible personnel involved, and punish them according to the law; (II) Publish the articles published in the Jiangsheng Daily supplement that Gu Zhutong considers to be "propagating communism"; (III) Effectively protect civil rights so as to ensure that similar facts do not happen again in the future.

DECLARATION OF THE SHANGHAI MUNICIPAL CHAMBER OF COMMERCE

Yesterday, an emergency meeting was held to submit a request to the central government for investigation and handling

A special committee for the Liu case was formed to be responsible for handling the matter

SHANGHAI JOURNALISTS ASSOCIATION

In response to Gu Zhutong's illegal execution of Liu Yusheng, the manager and editor of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, an emergency joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees was specially convened at the association's location at 4:00 p.m. yesterday. It was resolved to submit a request to the central government to severely punish Gu Zhutong. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded as follows:

ATTENDING MEMBERS

Jiang Jianhou, Jin Xiongbo, Gu Zhizhong, Li Zutan, Sun Daosheng, Jiang Zongdao, Tie Hua, Guo Butao, Wu Zhongyi, Jin Huating, Tang Huiping, Shen Qiuyan, Qian Cangshuo, Guan Jiu'an, Yan Esheng, Zhu Chaoran, Yu Kongwo, Qu Shaoyi, Zhao Junhao, Ma Chonggan

PROCEEDINGS OF THE MEETING

Chairman Yan Esheng, Recorder Wu Zhongyi, (A) The suggestion proposed by members Wu Zhongyi and 12 others, "Regarding Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Gu Zhutong's illegal execution of Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, to submit a request to the central government for strict handling in order to protect the rule of law," was discussed and passed. (I) All journalists in Shanghai will sign and issue a declaration; (II) The Journalists Association will submit a request to the Central Party Department and the National Government to investigate and handle Gu Zhutong; (III) A request will be submitted to the Supervisory Yuan to continue to impeach Gu Zhutong severely; (IV) The Newspaper Association, the Lawyers Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Education Association, and other legal organizations will jointly handle the matter; (V) A special committee for the Liu case will be established, and Yan Esheng, Qian Cangshuo, Qu Shaoyi, Wu Zhongyi, Yu Kongwo, Zhao Junhao, Shen Qiuyan, Du Gang, Jin Xiongbo, Qian Hua, Ma Chonggan and ten other people will be elected as members, to be convened by Yan Esheng; (VI) A declaration will be issued immediately; (VII) Hereafter, regarding news from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, anyone mentioning "Chairman Gu" will be referred to as Gu Zhutong.

ISSUING A DECLARATION

After the adjournment of the meeting, a special committee meeting was immediately convened to draft a declaration and decided to contact the journalists associations in Peiping, Tianjin, and Beijing to proceed jointly. The original text of the declaration is as follows: The Shanghai Journalists Association believes that in the case of Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, executing Liu Yusheng, manager and editor of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, the articles published in the newspaper's supplement "Iron Plough" cited by him had already been investigated and clarified by Supervisory Yuan supervisors Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin. They were merely works depicting the state of social life in China and there was no doubt that they did not promote communism or incite class struggle. Gu Zhutong arrested Liu Yusheng and imprisoned him for five months. After being impeached by the Supervisory Yuan and ordered by the Executive Yuan to transfer him to the court for trial, he executed him. The cited laws and regulations were also inconsistent. He violated the Provisional Constitution of the Tutelage Period, despised the highest supervisory authority, trampled on human rights, and disregarded human life. Such behavior was rare even in the warlord era, and unheard of after the party rule. Gu Zhutong dared to take the risk and brazenly did so. This association, in order to respect the law and protect human rights, must rise up and make a serious protest so that those who destroy the law and disrupt discipline will be sanctioned by law. This case is not only related to the safety of the news industry and the protection of journalists, but also endangers the freedom and survival of the people of the whole country. All citizens should condemn it together. This is our declaration.

ORIGINAL PROPOSAL

Regarding Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Gu Zhutong illegally executing Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, to submit a request to the central government for strict handling in order to uphold the rule of law. It is investigated that the Jiangsu Provincial Government executed Liu Yusheng, manager and editor of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, on January 21. According to the crimes reported by Gu Zhutong, chairman of the provincial government, in the provincial government's memorial week on the 23rd, the texts published in the newspaper's supplement were full of reactionary meaning and incited class struggle. The Military Commission approved the death penalty. According to the impeachment memorial of Supervisory Committee members Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin, the provincial government ordered the Provincial Public Security Bureau to shut down the Jiangsheng Daily and secretly summoned Liu Yusheng to the government, claiming that the newspaper violated the Publication Law and detained him for five months. Since he was not transferred to the court according to the law, he was renamed to be arbitrarily entering and exiting according to the provincial capital's martial law regulations, which obviously had other effects. As for the novels published in the supplement, they are merely works depicting the state of social life in China. What is the content and what is the accuracy of the observation? I will not discuss it for the time being. The Provisional Constitution of the Tutelage Period is to be observed by all levels of the country, and there are special articles on the protection of the people, and there are also special laws on the protection and banning of publications and speech. The responsibility of abiding by the law does not only belong to the people. What is Liu Yusheng's life and character like, and whether he has committed a crime punishable by death, are not what we want to hear. However, he was sentenced to death only because of the novels published in the newspaper's supplement, and he can be executed without trial in court. This is an unparalleled evil example in ancient and modern times, at home and abroad. Once a local official can arbitrarily make up charges and destroy the law for his own benefit, how can the people do anything? This association fights for human rights for the people of the hall and seeks protection for the news industry. It should rise up to strive for this and immediately submit a request to the central government to strictly handle the chairman Gu Zhutong's duties in order to warn others and uphold the rule of law. Please make a public decision.

JIANGSU PROVINCIAL GOVERNMENT'S REPLY TO THE EXECUTIVE YUAN

Accuses the "Iron Plough" supplement of inciting red terror

Believes that treasonous propaganda is punishable by death according to law

JIANGSU PROVINCIAL GOVERNMENT

Regarding the arrest of Liu Yusheng, the manager of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, the Supervisory Yuan submitted an impeachment case, and after the Executive Yuan's instruction arrived at the province, the provincial government has already enumerated the facts and legal principles in a memorial to the Executive Yuan yesterday (31st). The original text is as follows:

ORIGINAL REPLY

"Regarding the matter of replying to the memorial, the instruction No. 368 of the Executive Yuan states that the Supervisory Yuan's consultation No. 42 states that Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, illegally arrested and detained Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily, and the Yuan sent personnel to investigate, and again resisted, etc. A case of impeachment was filed. At that time, the Supervisory Yuan dispatched supervisors Zhou Lisheng, Gao Yihan, and Li Menggeng to review it. According to the report, it should be subject to disciplinary action and the Executive Yuan should be consulted to order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to promptly transfer Liu Yusheng to the court, etc. According to this, in addition to reporting to the National Government, the relevant documents in the original case are inspected and consulted to your Yuan for reference and handling, etc. Comply with the investigation and the Communist Party member Liu Yusheng was arrested last year. After interrogation by the Martial Law Command, it was clear that he was a Communist Party member. The seditious words in the newspaper were proved to have been written by himself. It was also clear that the criminal had joined Communist Party members in March of the sixteenth year to organize illegal trade unions and incite rickshaw pullers to strike, intending to disturb public order. The Political Department of the Second Division of the 17th Army of the National Revolutionary Army arrested and dealt with him. Although he took the opportunity to escape, his intention to plot rebellion has not stopped. As evidenced by the "Iron Plough" supplement, there are sentences such as "Our country's soldiers retreated to the left, and naturally the enemy came up to the right," "A red tide rose on the ground," and "Let the slaves fight, the era has swept up a storm, everything old will be overthrown immediately," "The era has struck a death knell, and everything old will be buried before our eyes," "Let the slaves fight," etc. His intention to incite class struggle and promote red terror is completely undisguised. After the January 28th Incident last year, Jiangsu was experiencing social and economic panic, people were uneasy, and the activities of bandits and communists were a hidden danger. There was always the risk of disturbances occurring. The government was trying to suppress the situation in order to eliminate the danger before it happened. The criminal took the opportunity to use the newspaper to incite the people, and it was obviously a deliberate act of treason. After interrogation by the Martial Law Command, the criminal was sentenced to death according to Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing those who Endanger the Republic of China. The matter was presented to the Martial Law Committee for approval and execution by shooting. The execution was carried out by the Martial Law Command on January 21. The presentation was reported to your Yuan by this government in No. 17, and reported to the Military Commission in separate reports. Now, the sections forwarded by the Supervisory Yuan are hereby presented to your Yuan for reference. As for the circumstances mentioned in the attachments to the consultation from the Supervisory Yuan, the application of the Publication Law to control newspapers, the application of the Martial Law Regulations to try criminals, and the authority of the Martial Law Command to handle trials within the martial law area are all based on laws and regulations. They have not been able to appreciate the situation and blame each other with ordinary legal principles and peacetime conditions. This is inconsistent with the situation in Jiangsu Province after the January 28th Incident. As for the Supervisory Yuan's access to files, whether it can be applied to events in which the electrical affairs organ tries criminals is a major question. Because the power of the organ cannot be arbitrarily expanded by the organ itself. Moreover, the crimes of communist party members endanger the country. A slight lack of caution can cause changes. We should all have the same understanding and not be swayed by personal emotions, which would be fortunate for the future of the country. Jointly presented, respectfully presented to the Executive Yuan."

DUAN QIRUI FIRMLY DENIES NEWSPAPER RUMORS

Regarding the so-called "Pan-Asianism"

He does not know what it is at all

Zhang Xiaoruo and Zhang Renkui paid their respects yesterday

According to the Central News Agency, all Japanese newspapers in Shanghai carried a dispatch from the Electric Communication Agency in Tokyo the day before yesterday, stating that China, Russia, Japan, and "Manchuria" will carry out cooperation to realize "Pan-Asianism." On the Chinese side, Duan Qirui has obtained understanding. Duan Qirui has strongly advocated this theory before Chairman Chiang and Zhang Xueliang, etc. In front of this news item, a huge headline was added to sensationalize the audience. A Central News Agency reporter specially visited Duan Qirui at the World Academy yesterday to inquire about the truth of the so-called "Pan-Asianism." Duan Qirui immediately firmly denied this statement. Duan Qirui not only does not have the idea of ​​China, Russia, Japan and Manchuria" cooperating, but also does not know what the so-called "Pan-Asianism" is at all. Duan Qirui came south this time for private affairs and has no political opinions. As for Duan Qirui's views on the Sino-Japanese issue, he firmly advocates that the Japanese side must first return the Northeast to our country, and then there will be room for negotiations. Duan Qirui fundamentally denies the so-called "Manchukuo," and even more so that there is no possibility of cooperation. The so-called "Pan-Asianism" is obviously a fabricated rumor by the Japanese side to confuse the hearing of people all over the world. Duan Qirui hopes that the people of the country will recognize the cunning of the Japanese and not be deceived. Duan Qirui believes that the World Academy where he lives is a cultural institution and is inconvenient to live in for a long time, so he is looking for another house and will move within a week. Yesterday at noon, Songhu Garrison Commander Guan Ji and Staff Officer Zhang Xiang hosted a banquet for Duan at the East Asia Restaurant. Duan was too tired from socializing for days and was very tired, so he did not attend the banquet. The Anhui Association in Shanghai is scheduled to hold a joint banquet for Duan on the 4th at noon in conjunction with various Anhui industry associations in Shanghai.

Yesterday afternoon, Zhang Xiaoruo went to see Duan Zhilao and was received. He inquired about the handling of industry, education and self-government in Nantong in recent years. RUSSIAN EMBASSY IN CHINA DECIDES TO TEMPORARILY ESTABLISH SHANGHAI

According to the Shanghai News Agency, the following news was obtained from the Soviet People's Association in Shanghai and the diplomatic circles in our country after the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union.

The Russian Embassy decided to temporarily establish Shanghai. According to the news from the Soviet Russian Overseas Chinese Association in Shanghai, the Russian Embassy in China has now decided to temporarily establish Shanghai. After Losky arrives, because various treaties between China and Russia are urgently awaiting negotiation, in order to facilitate the negotiation, he also decided to stay in Shanghai. As for the embassy building, the association is currently looking for it. In the future, the Consulate General will be attached to the embassy to save expenses. Although the candidate for the Consul General in Shanghai has not yet been officially announced by the Soviet Russian government, according to the observations of the Soviet Russian Overseas Chinese Association and the opinions of the majority of Russian overseas Chinese, it is still hoped that Haweid, the Deputy Consul in Shanghai before the severance of diplomatic relations, can be reappointed. Therefore, the Soviet Russian Overseas Chinese Association has telegraphed the government requesting permission to appoint Haweid as Consul General in Shanghai to meet the expectations of the public.

Our side restores consulates in Russia. According to reliable information from the diplomatic circles in Shanghai, since our diplomatic authorities announced the resumption of diplomatic relations with Russia, they have been actively preparing to restore consulates in various parts of Russia. As of today, a total of thirteen consulates have been announced, including Moscow, Vladivostok, Luohe, Boli, Irkutsk, Tashkent, Chita, Shuangchengzi, Troba, Almaty, Anjiyan, Zaisang, Xie Mi, etc. As for the Deputy Consuls in the above-mentioned places, those who have been officially appointed by the Foreign Ministry include the Consul of the Moscow Consulate Case Qing, the Consul General of Vladivostok Xu Xiongzhang, the Deputy Consul Liu Yuying, the Consul General of Heihe Quan Shien, the Deputy Consul Huang Yuding, the Consul General of Jianli Guan Shangping, the Deputy Consul Bao Gu, the Consul of Irkutsk Zhu Beixin, the Consul General of Tashkent Mou Shan, the Deputy Consul Liu Deen, the Consul General of Chita Tan Kuang, the Consul of Shuanchengzi Zhang Rang, the Consul General of Shuangchengzi Gu Wenhua, the Deputy Consul Sun Wendou, the Consul General of Troba Gou Zengshu, the Consul General of Almaty Ba Guoxin, the Consul General of Anjiyan Yan Shuen, the Consul General of Zaisang Guanglu, the Consul General of Shuanchengzi Ma Wanlu, the Consul General of Xie Mi Xie Guosong, etc. Twenty people

Thirty security guards arrived in Shanghai. Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union, the Soviet Russian government, in order to prevent the Russian household in China from plotting sabotage, decided that before Losky, the first ambassador to China after the resumption of diplomatic relations, took office, it would first send 30 security guards to China to protect the Soviet Russian business institutions and diplomatic residences in Shanghai. This security guard team has arrived in Shanghai from Vladivostok on a Norwegian merchant ship a few days ago and is temporarily stationed there to perform its tasks. Once Losky arrives in Shanghai, it will also organize a plainclothes reconnaissance team to investigate the actions of the Russian household in every possible way to maintain the safety of the Soviet citizens in Shanghai.

AFTER THE SHANGHAI COUNTY MOVES ITS SEAT OF GOVERNMENT

The security of Beiqiao is extremely consolidated

The local area shows signs of development

The Shanghai County has implemented the relocation to Beiqiao Town, which has been completed. Now all the staff are engaged in internal sorting and arrangement in addition to daily official duties. Because all the items have been transported from the county office, it will take some time to arrange them properly. The county office building is more magnificent than the old office. The office of the county head's secretary is in the center of the main building. The Finance Bureau is in the east building, and the county government office is in the west building. The Construction Bureau is in the east of the lower floor, and the Education Bureau is in the west. All organs and groups are in one breath. The new money and grain counter to the east of the county office can be fully completed immediately. The area around the county office is still farmland, but it is gradually transforming into a residential area. Because there have never been any theft cases in the Beiqiao area, security has become more consolidated after the relocation. The land is located at the intersection of the Shanghai-Min and Bei-Hui motorways, between Songjiang and Shanghai. There are frequent car trips every day, and transportation is convenient. It is only half an hour's drive to Shanghai, and the cost of living is not as high as in Shanghai, which has attracted the attention of general residents. Moreover, schools have purchased school bases there one after another, and are preparing to start construction of school buildings one after another this year. In the future, when the schools move, the material needs will increase, and the number of stores and their business will inevitably increase. Among the schools that purchase land, the Law and Politics University has the widest land, about nearly one hundred acres. The second is Guanghua Experimental Middle School and Xinhua Art College, each with about 20 acres. The authorities of each school have different amounts of land. The authorities of each school intend to purchase land here. On the one hand, the land price is only one-tenth of that of the quiet areas in the center of Shanghai. On the other hand, the area is quiet, suitable for chanting, and the transportation is convenient, so there is no feeling of hardship. However, although the land price there is cheap, since the schools purchased the land, the average price per mu has doubled compared to the past.

Books, etc. arrived in Shanghai yesterday

According to the Central News Agency, the Geological Institute and the Institute of Language and History of the Academia Sinica, which are located in Peiping, have been ordered by the academy to move south. THE SINO-BRITISH BOXER INDEMNITY FUND APPROVES THE RAILWAY MINISTRY'S PUBLIC DEBT GUARANTEE

Refers to three items of income such as freight surcharges

Still waiting for the general meeting to be approved on the 6th of this month

Yesterday, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee held a finance committee meeting at 2 p.m. at No. 1 Bing, Jiujiang Road, to review the guarantee issue for the Railway Ministry's proposed issuance of £1.2 million in public debt for the completion of the Yuehan Railway. Attending were Chairman Rong Fu, Hua Shiye, Xi Dong Kang Deli, Finance Committee members Chen Cai, Song Ziwen, Xi Committee member Maxwell, Director General Hang Liwu, Family Adviser Ren Chuanbang, and Railway Ministry representatives Sa Fujun and Huang Zhensheng, etc. The discussion lasted for four hours and did not end until about 6 p.m. As a result, the review work of the Finance Committee has come to an end. Regarding the guarantee issue, it was approved to use the current surcharges on passenger and freight transportation on various railways under the Ministry of Railways, as well as the three items of income from the Capital Ferry and the Guangshao section of the Yuehan Railway, as guarantees for the issuance of public debt, and it was decided that the committee would prepare a report and submit it to the general meeting to be held in Shanghai on the 6th of this month for discussion and approval. In addition, the board of directors also approved the convocation of a standing committee meeting on the 4th of this month to discuss association affairs.

MUNICIPAL CHAMBER OF COMMERCE TELEGRAM REQUESTS NEGOTIATION ON VIETNAM'S RE-IMPOSITION OF BOOK TAXES

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Education yesterday, stating, "Respectfully to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Education in Nanjing, we received a letter from the Book Industry Association on the 31st of this month stating, 'It is found that book accessories are common in China and foreign countries, and elementary school textbooks in particular have many illustrations to arouse children's interest. We have never heard of them being regarded as books. However, according to the report of the Meiqun Printing Bureau in Dike, Vietnam, the books shipped from our country to Vietnam this time, including the Basic Primary School Social Studies textbooks Volumes 1 and 2, Basic Elementary School Arithmetic textbooks Volume 2, Kindergarten Readers, Kindergarten Numeracy, Basic Elementary School Art textbooks, etc., were forcibly designated as books by the customs and had to pay heavy taxes, and were also charged with tax evasion penalties and detained.' It is found that the import of books and books is tax-free, and the customs release them. This time, the French Vietnamese customs forcibly designated textbooks as books, levied heavy taxes, which is harmful to the culture of overseas Chinese in Vietnam, and is especially unfair to the Sino-French reciprocal trade agreement. In addition to presenting this to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for examination and requesting a prompt negotiation with the French ambassador, please order the government of Annam to release the detained books on the one hand and strictly verify the customs so as not to consider textbooks as books. In addition to this, we respectfully request your association to examine and grant assistance, and we are looking forward to it.' It is found that the circumstances of this case are clearly the difficulties of the Vietnamese customs officials, who deliberately changed the items when collecting taxes, which is not an increase in the tax rate. Therefore, after checking the circumstances, it is not much related to the case of reciprocal goods items not yet being signed. At this time, our country's consul in Vietnam has not been appointed, and there are no officials nearby who can handle negotiations. The only thing to do is to telegraph your ministry to forward a letter to the French ambassador, asking the Vietnamese Governor of the country to earnestly obstruct it, and still tax according to the book law, return the detained goods, and stop Zhaogongdao. We are eagerly awaiting orders, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce".
