K> Spring and Autumn

Ice Talk

— Zhanlu

Gusts of north wind harden the soft and warm water of Jiangnan. Do you say it "flows east when directed east, flows west when directed west"? It actually fiercely battles the hardened north wind, "It is easier to shake a mountain than to shake a harbor frozen with ice!" The more tightly the north wind presses, the more solid the position becomes, as unshakeable as steel and iron! It is a tough guy, a desperate resister! It can deal with the harsh north wind, but it cannot deal with the gentle spring breeze. With just a slight breeze, hey! It cannot control itself! Like a Chu song scattering the 8,000 soldiers of Xiang Yu, the solid group dissolves! Its attitude changes! It is no longer ice but water! Its face rises and falls with the wind! It can become a whirlpool or a ripple as it pleases. It is a weakling! It is a believer in non-resistance! Alas! Where has the tough attitude of before gone?

In the moment when drops of water first freeze into ice, all the bottles, pots, jars, hair, and scattered glassware are like corrupt officials, big and small, who, upon hearing the order to investigate, quickly try to smuggle out the ill-gotten gains they have embezzled! All the water stored in their bellies expresses their innate and utterly clean nature through vomiting, spitting, pouring, and emptying. If the vomiting and emptying are delayed for even a moment, hey! How terrible! Once the embezzled goods expand, even the seven-stone jar that boasts "greatness within" will burst its big belly into three or five pieces! I wish to make that shattered seven-stone jar a mirror for corrupt officials.

I do not smoke water pipes, dry pipes, or any tobacco. However, an old gentleman in the same room hugs this white metal water pipe like Zhaoyun carrying A Dou. I hear him muttering to himself, "In such cold weather, everyone is shrinking their necks and not raising their heads, but you are raising your head? Aren't you afraid of the cold? Don't you need to wear an otter fur coat and a woolen scarf?" I ask strangely, "Old brother, who is raising their head there?" He answers with a smile, "My water pipe is frozen. The foolish, wife-like pipe head is extending its neck half an inch higher than usual."

The Gathering of the Masses

— Ren Ying

Around the Great World during the Lunar New Year

This area is usually bustling, but it becomes even more so during the Lunar New Year. Groups of laborers who sell their labor can get three or four days of rest. Near the Great World, crowds surge like waves. They spend the whole year depleting their blood and strength, and now they are searching for the precious entertainment that they have for a few days, like dew in the desert.

The cement ground opposite the Great World is filled with teams of Shandong performers. There are peep shows that have been exposed, puppet shows inside blue cloth curtains, strange cries, and rhythmic gongs. Outside the circle, groups of people crane their necks and wait. The iron gates in front of the Great World have already been pulled shut; they are probably putting on a show of being full. A group of prostitutes waiting for customers in the cold night wind are gradually appearing. Red robes, green jackets, white face powder, red rouge – in the eyes of the laboring masses, these are objects of sexual pursuit. But in the eyes of the city's young masters, these are terrifying demons. A group of bored hooligans throw firecrackers wrapped in colored paper at the feet of ladies. Resentful faces are exchanged for the hooligans' ferocious smiles.

The game of three cards also appears on the side of the road. There are gentle shouts and the clinking of silver coins. A group of people crowd around the wooden stall, and friends wearing peaked caps and leggings guard the outside of the circle. Some middle-aged women put a copper coin into the container for the fortune-telling sticks of the God of Wealth. Passing by several store entrances, I see them pasted with peach-colored Spring Festival couplets. The sound of the New Year drum, which I loved to hear as a child, ripples out from the door seams. Looking westward, a bright red setting sun reflects the blood flowers of the January 28th Incident martyrs.

Taking Pictures

— Mo Yi

In the weather outside the customs, there is almost no difference between autumn and winter; the scorching summer is driven away by the bleak autumn wind, and the unique northwest wind of winter roars like a knife scraping needles. The sky-filled yellow sand rolls in the sky like waves in the ocean; and the snowflakes hidden in the layers of dark clouds, after a few days of northwest wind, when the mercury on the thermometer drops below zero, it sweeps away the yellow sand and dances in the air. A thick layer of snow accumulates on the ground, first frozen by the northwest wind, as if covering the ground with a layer of marble, and then the sky clears, and the warm sun shoots out its heat, harmonizing the air everywhere, and the snow melts, and it is simply impossible to insert a foot on the muddy road; but when the sun is forced away by the night, or another layer of snow is added, it freezes again, and it freezes and melts alternately, until the original ground can be seen in March and April of the following year.

One morning after four or five days of heavy snow, the sun climbed up from the horizon, not with the usual smile, and the faint sunlight seemed to be worried about its appearance. The people in Lizigou Village, Fushun County, did not dare to sleep because they heard gunfire and shouting all night last night. When they got up early this morning, their faces were full of surprised expressions, and they gathered in twos and threes to guess the source of the gunfire and shouting last night.

"Didn't you all sleep last night?" Zhang Rongjiu sat on the porch of his house with his neighbors Wang Fugen and Zhao Da, basking in the sun, and said, flicking off the ashes from his cigarette.

"How dare I sleep! Didn't you hear gunfire all night! What about you?" Wang Fugen lit a cigarette and took two strong puffs.

"It was so lively all night, and I don't know what happened?" Zhao Da stared at the circles of smoke coming out of Wang Fugen's nostrils and mouth and said.

"I think it must be the Volunteer Army fighting the dwarves all night again!"

"That's right. I don't know how the victory or defeat is?"

"By the way, weren't there three ......" Zhao Da said as if he remembered something. Halfway through, he saw a stranger limping in, stepping on the slightly melting snow, and didn't say anything else.

"Please ... ... please ... ... you ... ... me ... ... for a while, oh ... ... it hurts ... ... it hurts oh ... ..." the sudden man shouted with a pale face and gritted teeth, very painfully.

The three of them stood up together, ran over to help the man, and sat him down on the porch. The three of them stood around him. (One)

Miscellaneous Notes

Nine-Flavor Tea

— Zhang Yian

We Cantonese people have a kind of medicine called "Nine-Flavor Tea." It's made of many odds and ends of medicines combined together, including even old cow dung and broken bowls. (This is the truth.) Strictly speaking, a complete dose of Nine-Flavor Tea has more than nine ingredients, so it is also known as "Odds-and-Ends Tea." But the original Nine-Flavor Tea probably only had nine ingredients, and it was gradually increased by later additions.

It is said that this Nine-Flavor Tea can cure many ailments, especially colds, indigestion, and so on. According to my experience, it is often quite effective for intestinal problems, but it may not work for other problems. The medicine is not formulated by famous doctors or experts, and many of its ingredients are not found in the Materia Medica, and it is so miscellaneous. Sometimes it works, sometimes it doesn't, and the taste is bitter and unpleasant. I think it is quite similar to this article of mine, so I took it as the name. Although this article is as miscellaneous as Nine-Flavor Tea, I don't guarantee that its usefulness is equivalent. I hereby declare this in advance.

It is very disappointing when a burst of joy suddenly cannot be realized. Indeed, people should always strive towards their desired goals, one step at a time, and should not be discouraged by any failures. I myself have been fooled by hope many times... After giving it my best effort, the result often dissipated like a soap bubble. Having had such experiences many times, I am no longer so daring to trust hope. Hope exists, but I don't dare to expect it to have the result that I have predetermined. Just do my best to do it, and don't necessarily be discouraged. When the time comes, whatever the result, just let it be. For example, when planning whether to succeed at the time, obstacles of time and people must be expected to occur. If you can consider this in advance, you can reduce a lot of disappointment and sadness at the time. This attitude seems close to the indifference of middle age and the loss of the vigor of youth. But experience tells you to do so, so why should you force yourself to go against nature and deceive yourself? Experience is the most scientific. (Mao Dun's "Disillusionment" seems to describe this kind of mentality.)

When I arrived in Wuxi, I got some impressions:

A friend who had lived there for a few months accompanied us on our tour and tried to show off his knowledge of Wuxi everywhere. For example, when hiring rickshaws, he deliberately negotiated the price down to the lowest possible amount for us. In fact, we may not be ignorant of the things he wanted to show off.

Perhaps because I was thirsty, I found the tea brewed with Huiquan water particularly delicious. If Huiquan water is really so good, I must bring a dozen or so thermos bottles to transport some back to Shanghai next time.

Two rickshaw pullers fought with their fists against their colleagues for a ride. This may be a small symbol of the struggle for survival.

It is rare to have new experiences sitting at home. If you want to get some new experiences, you must go out the door, the farther the better.

The smell of the sun scorching the wild grass is something that people in the city cannot smell. Most of them only smell coal smoke.

Because the rickshaw puller was rushing to grab business, he pulled the wrong rickshaw of a colleague, and was caught up by that rickshaw puller, which delayed me and made me fall behind.

In the city park, there were slogans in large black characters on white "foreign" cloth, and paper strips that were still posted saying "Guest Registration" and "Ladies' Reception." Several workers were moving chairs out of the park, and part of the park was obviously a bit messy. I thought this must be a meeting of some kind, and the meeting period had already passed, and this was a scene after the meeting. The next day, I learned from the newspaper that a certain member of the party and a certain lady held their wedding ceremony there. So I said you must go out and see to get new experiences.

Ke Xian Prices Fall and Sales are Brisk

Price Drops Another Small Jiao... Minhua Exceptionally Prosperous

Yesterday, the arrival of Ke Xian was not prosperous. Because various producing areas heard that national circulation did not require passport fees, people's hearts were uplifted, and they all collected and hoarded. Therefore, the production price was instead firm and it was difficult to make profitable sales. However, in Shanghai, foreign rice and Du rice squeezed each other's feet, and the market was difficult to improve for a while. Moreover, Du rice downstream can be circulated to various ports across the country starting yesterday, without unnecessary procedures such as passports. Since rice from downstream can circulate smoothly, the market for Ke rice will inevitably be squeezed. Because rice merchants from Hunan and Jiangxi are all strongly advocating for early disposal, they no longer hold the attitude of guarding it like last winter. After the market opened in the morning, each Xian depreciated by a small jiao across the board. After the price decreased, the Min gang immediately handled it briskly. Local merchants and hoarders also took the opportunity to inquire, and the market became active. The overall market was handled by the Fuzhou gang from Fujian Province, going to Jiangxi with 1,270 packages of late machine rice, 800 packages of Hunan machine red rice, 500 packages of Hunan oil rice. Furthermore, Quanzhou sent 1,000 packages of Hunan oil rice. The local scattered households sent over 1,000 packages of Hunan oil rice and 300 packages of red rice. Hunan machine oil rice was priced from 9 yuan 1 jiao 7 fen to 8 yuan 9 jiao, and machine red rice was priced from 8 yuan 7 jiao 5 fen to 8 yuan 6 jiao 5 fen. Jiangxi machine late rice was priced from 8 yuan 9 jiao 5 fen to 8 yuan 8 jiao 5 fen, it is said.

Oil Market

Overview of Cottonseed Oil Factory Operations Last Year

Cooperation Effective in the First Half, Rapeseed Concurrently Operated in the Second Half

Dayou, Dachang, etc., Each Had Surpluses of 30,000 to 56,000

The number of cottonseed oil pressing factories in this port is only six or seven, but the raw material demand has always been greater than the supply. Last year, the number of cotton blossoms was poor, and the output was not strong. Cottonseed was even more in short supply. Fortunately, on the import side, the industry cooperated to jointly establish a raw material procurement office to purchase. The prices were also determined by the office according to the market, so the cottonseed price did not jump out of line. The oil cakes were stable due to the limited output. Therefore, although the oil factory operations in the first half of last year were affected by the Shanghai war, they were able to avoid significant losses due to the industry cooperation. Last autumn, the harvest of cotton blossoms was quite abundant, but the new factory Hengxingtai was established as a non-member, becoming an opponent to the procurement office. This was because many of the factory's shareholders were flower-ginning factories in Pudong. Therefore, after its establishment, Pudong cottonseed was almost completely monopolized. The amount of cotton used in Pudong accounts for 20% of the total amount used by each factory, and therefore, the factories suffered from a shortage of goods again. The factory machines could not be fully operated and only produced oil cakes to maintain operations. As a result, the factories faced difficulties in producing oil cakes, and Dayou took the lead in producing rapeseed to maintain operations. According to this settlement, Dayou and Dachang, etc., each had surpluses ranging from 10,000 to 56,000. It is said that they profited from producing rapeseed. The other factories barely broke even. Because of its superior position, Shanghai Oil also had a surplus of 30,000 yuan.

Business Sutra (II)

Doors for Acquiring Western Suits

Western Suits

。Because there are more stores, the pricing is relatively fair. It is important to pay attention and bargain. It is best to visit several stores to compare. After the sample is sold, pay the deposit slowly. First cut a small sample, and add to it the next day. In order to take samples to other stores for comparison. ㈡ When looking at the sample, be sure to recognize whose sample it is. You can take the small sample to that place to inquire. (A phone call is also fine.) When inquiring, be sure to first ask for the sample number with a discount. How many discounts are there in cash? Then how much money is needed for this clothing fabric? Even if you want to cheat, it will no longer be possible. Benefit tailors often overcalculate the material needed, profiting from it. To make a suit, in reality, you need two yards and seventy-five inches of material. They must say that they need three yards. Smart customers do not need to have them buy it for them. Buy the material yourself. At most, buy two yards and eight inches. Adding a little extra is enough. If you let the tailor buy it for you, they will not only want to make money, but also want to profit from the material. With each layer adding profit, the customer suffers twice. ㈣ If you find it troublesome to buy the material yourself, you can also go to the Xiaoximen, Daxin Street, and Wusong Road areas to buy ready-made goods. Because the area there is small and the expenses are less, business is more accommodating than in other places. Although the workmanship is slightly inferior, there should be a special difference, and the price is much cheaper. However, careful inspection is still essential.

Overcoats

For Western-style overcoats, of course, it is most appropriate to have them made at a Western-style clothing store. Because their style and workmanship are more beautiful than other overcoat workshops. For making Chinese-style overcoats, if you want to be economical, you can go to Daxin Street, Qipan Street, Wusong Road, and Xiaoximen areas to buy them. The prices are relatively cheaper. However, even though the price heard is cheap, you still need to bargain. It should be about several yuan. It is best to visit several stores to avoid being taken advantage of even in a cheap deal. After the price is agreed upon, specify what kind of goods the lining and interlining are. The lining can be satin or camel hair. The quality of the two is different, so you must choose carefully. Black charcoal interlining is the best. If not specified, Ningbo Jiangshan interlining will be used. Also, for a French-style interlining, do not use cloth lining. (Some dishonest stores will say it is French-style interlining when ordering, but change to using summer cloth lining and hemp sackcloth, etc., when making it.) The sleeve lining must be genuine silk. Horsehair interlining prices vary greatly between genuine and fake. Genuine goods sell for two yuan per yard, while fake goods only sell for six jiao. After everything is specified and a deal is made, you must take samples. (Note). The sample of the clothing material should be slightly larger, so that you can compare it with the finished clothing. Otherwise, sometimes the comparison will not be clear, and the store will cheat you, leaving you with no way to argue. If you buy the material yourself and give it to a tailor to make, the labor and parts will cost about thirteen or fourteen yuan per piece. (Including lining, interlining, pocket cloth, buttons, etc.) When buying the overcoat material, you must accurately calculate your length and size. If you are short, you cannot add more. If there is too much, it is good for the tailor, and it is not worth it. For example, if your height is three feet six or seven inches, you can cut two yards and eight inches of overcoat wool. If a robe is three feet eight or nine inches, you can cut three yards. Beyond four feet, you need three yards and one "gua du" (i.e., two inches and a half). This is all calculated using the latest style of "ben ku" sleeves. If it is the old-fashioned round sleeve, you can save one or two "jiao" of material.

Rulers

The rulers used by the industry to measure the length of cloth are mostly made by themselves. However, when necessary, you should still rely on the Deji, Huaji, and Tianyou rulers. Thirty-six inches is counted as one yard. Each yard is divided into ten "jiao." Each "jiao" is three inches and six points, totaling two inches and a half in the center. Two and a half "jiao" is called one "gua du" (Quarter) by Westerners. Seven and a half "jiao" is three "gua du", exactly twelve inches and seven and a half points, which is half a yard. (However, the cloth industry often says that two feet and six inches is one yard. In reality, it is measured by 98 feet when folding people's clothing.) Two feet and five and a half inches is one yard. Within a yard, there are still differences of 125, 25, 375, 625, and 75.

Free Talk

The Melting of Snow (2)

– Xu Jie

I knocked on the water surface, it only revealed some white flowers, it was almost harder than a stone slab. I shook the water tank, and there was no moving water at the bottom of the tank. As for the little fish, some of them were frozen white before being solidified; some were frozen quietly and motionless in mid-air, just like when they were swimming; and some had their little tails curved, showing a gesture of trying to turn around. However, everything was solidified, frozen. Moreover, everything was clearly and transparently displayed before my eyes, so that I could see clearly. I suddenly felt sad. I felt as if I was also frozen in this ice world, and I cried, I cried very sadly.

I think you can imagine this situation to some extent, even if you haven't experienced it! Gentlemen, in this weather, our bodies and souls are also frozen like this!

Take a look at the weather these past few days. Indeed, a few days ago, our eaves also dripped water, and the snow water was melting drop by drop, which made us feel quite energetic. However, the situation these past few days is clearly before our eyes. Isn't the snow water in front of our eaves melting a little and dripping a few drops during the day, only to refreeze again at night, and even have more snow added on top?

In the past few days, because some people were still making fires to keep warm, some people were chatting idly, and even because some people were still living and hadn't stopped breathing, a few drops of water could still drip during the day, indicating a sign that the snow would soon collapse. But now, even if some people are still making fires and breathing, they can't make the severe ice and snow disappear even a little. If this continues, wouldn't you think that even fires won't start in the future? Wouldn't you think that even your breath will be frozen, and you won't be able to exhale freely anymore?

Of course, we know that spring and warmth, which will save us from the misfortune of this harsh winter, will arrive sooner or later. However, in today's world, where both body and soul are frozen in ice and snow, it is very difficult to endure even a minute or a second. Moreover, in these anxious days of waiting for spring to arrive, we will feel particularly that these days are hard to get through, and we may even suspect that spring will never come. Friends, please imagine, in my little fish, the few little fish that froze to death in the snow, in their posture of struggling with their tails curved, in their relaxed posture of stretching their chests and evenly balancing their limbs, did they ever think that spring would eventually come?

This is the truth. Even if spring really arrives one day, our current lives will not be able to last until spring, so what then? If spring only arrives after your own life has ended, do you believe that spring has arrived, or has it never arrived?

Melting snow is colder than falling snow. What's more, the current snow is melting and falling again, melting and falling again, and it has been completely frozen together, with ice on the snow and snow on the ice!

The weather like this is indeed extremely severe, but it is not appropriate to just wait and be frozen in this frozen world, unable to breathe. We Chinese have an old saying, "Everyone sweeps the snow in front of their own door." I think we should do the work of sweeping the snow in front of our own doors ourselves! We still need to do some snow-sweeping work, we need to stretch our breath a little.

Ah, "Melting snow is colder than falling snow," what harsh weather!

January 5, 1933

George Bernard Shaw and John Galsworthy

— Yu Dafu

We were preparing to warmly welcome the long-faced prophet Old Shaw, but unfortunately, we received the obituary of last year's Nobel Prize winner, John Galsworthy. Shaw is seventy-six years old this year. Galsworthy was sixty-five years old this year.

In principle, sixty-five years old is not considered a premature death, but if this precise recorder of the British upper class, who came from a legal background, had not died, he might have produced several more masterpieces in the future to report to us on the shaking and changes of the British upper class. Galsworthy's literary achievements are not only the Forsyte Saga, but also the Silver Box, Strife, Justice, and The Mob, which will be immortalized. Even his discovery of the naval writer Conrad during a trip to the South Seas in 1893 should occupy a place in the history of English literature. Although he came from a relatively upper-class background, his attitude of always speaking for humanity and criticizing society is one that we must give full respect even in this era of changing times and turbulent tides.

Conversely, Shaw's attitude toward society is different. At first, it seems that he is just joking and not taking things seriously, but after closing your eyes and thinking, or after laughing and turning your mind, you can immediately discover that every joke and scolding of this long-faced old man is a shot in the arm aimed at the crux of society. Well said, Joseph McCabe, who criticized Shaw, saying, "He does not say epigrams, but he himself is an epigram. He is the most moral immoralist, the most altruistic egoistic preacher, the purest denier of the Ten Commandments, and the most serious humorist." Isn't this a very appropriate assessment of Shaw?

Once, an actress famous in Europe and America for her beauty said to him, "Mr. Shaw, if you marry me and have a child, with my appearance and your brains, wouldn't that child be the most beautiful and intelligent person in the world?" Shaw said, "What if the appearance looks like mine and the brains look like yours? That would be terrible!"

Countless witty remarks like this have been made during Shaw's seventy-six years. I remember when he went to Russia for a visit, even Stalin had to acknowledge him as a junior of Marxism, because he said, "I studied Marx long before Lenin." At that time, the capitalist countries of Europe were publicizing the inhumane forced labor of Soviet Russia, but Shaw said to the Russians, "I wish that such inhumane phenomena would occur in Europe and America, otherwise, where would those millions of unemployed workers find a way out?"

Fortunately, we in China still have Mr. Lu Xun, who can be compared with George Bernard Shaw. People are scolding him for using the old trick of the Shaoxing scribe to kill people with a few words, but George Bernard Shaw is not from Jingshan, is he? February 1, 1932.

Quick Sketch on the Shanghai-Wuxi Route

— Huang Zengrong

"Finally, I see smoke!" So, the people standing at the bottom seemed to have taken an stimulant. They yawned, stretched their waists, and each picked up their belongings, preparing for the upcoming squeeze. The women were still cursing the train's delay, which had made them wait for two hours.

The police also began to work. They carried wooden sticks and stood on the platforms on both sides of the tracks, warning people to step back a little. Occasionally, when they encountered one or two ignorant villagers, hum! The wooden sticks would be applied to their bodies and say an unlucky sentence: "Looking for death?"

The train rushed into the platform. It was not easy to squeeze into the third-class carriage, but it was already full of people standing. A gentleman in a suit was lying comfortably sideways. According to the people next to him, this gentleman came from Zhenjiang, maybe it was for "official business," or maybe he was an "important person"! Wasn't he? He was also pillowing a "official business briefcase" under his head! So everyone dared not argue with him, because they knew, "Official business" is always "official business," and "important people" are always "important people"!

The train was approaching Hushu Pass, and the ticket inspector came, followed by two military policemen, who were also very imposing. Oh! China's military police are only good enough to follow people and check tickets!

When the ticket inspector came to the lying gentleman, he put on a very solemn look and told him to get up. Of course, the gentleman in the suit would not submit. The ticket inspector's reason was quite sufficient, he said,

"If you don't get up, you will have to pay for two more tickets." Indeed, he was simply occupying the space of three people. The gentleman in the suit finally sat up, probably because he didn't want to pay for the extra tickets. However, in order to save his own face, after the ticket inspector left, he looked at the ticket inspector's back and cursed, "Damn it." This was of course blaming the ticket inspector for not opening his eyes and not taking his "official business briefcase" seriously.

How uncomfortable the train was! The smoke was thick, it was really suffocating. An unknown gentleman said,

"Ah... smoking is really unhygienic!"

But the smokers glared at him.

The train went straight past Nanxiang! Of course, I felt more relieved in my heart. However, the smoke all around, mixed with the congestion of carbon dioxide exhaled by more than a hundred people, made me feel even more nervous and temporarily uncomfortable. Fortunately! Shanghai is almost here!

Shanghai has finally arrived! Ha! Finally arrived! I quickly jumped out of the carriage, as if I were a prisoner who had been pardoned.

Model Collective Market

— Native

From carrots to all sorts of things, a collective market like a glass palace, opened in Moscow in early October last year. This collective market is very outstanding. There is a nursery where people who go shopping can entrust their children. There is a rest room, a restaurant, ventilation equipment, a sanitary drinking fountain, and fire protection devices. As long as the sprinkler heads, which are very technically installed in the roof and walls, are turned on, any part of this large building will not be affected by other parts.

It is estimated that this first model collective market in Moscow can accommodate 8,000 customers at a time. Eighty-one stalls specialize in selling food from collective farms and state farms. A 300-meter-long counter sells various peasant products, from food to embroidered work clothes. In addition, there is a 200-meter-long counter that specializes in clothes, shoes, fabrics, and exquisite utensils. A doctor is always on site. Veterinarians and agricultural experts will inspect all the food sold.

The front of this novel building is decorated with statues of a man and a woman, leaning against an overturned basket, from which an endless stream of horticultural products flows. In front of this large building is a lawn with gardens and fountains.

Ulianiski, the person in charge of the construction, said that construction began on July 20, with an average of 450 people working on it every day. Since the start of construction, the construction plan has been changed, so the cost has increased from the budgeted 750,000 rubles to nearly 1.2 million rubles, and the scheduled time has been extended to complete this great work.

Long Form Creation

The Crossroads of the Era and Love (Continued)

— Zhang Ziping

"Just flipping through it a bit, not doing any deep research. Mr. Lin, you like reading novels, don't you?"

"I want to create. Because art is a symbol of distress... so when Shirakaba Kuson advocated it, some people quickly imported it."

"But, Mr. Lin, in modern times, that's no longer a fashionable slogan."

She said, tilting her head slightly, smiling as if amused.

"Ah, ah."

He felt his face getting hot. He wanted to ask her what she meant by "slogan," but he felt that if he asked, she would look down on him, so he just reacted with "Ah, ah," waiting for her to continue.

"Mr. Lin, how do you think literature and art should be defined?"

"Literature and art are a reflection of society."

He answered her very quickly. He thought this would definitely win her external applause and internal admiration. But he still felt a little ashamed inside. Because this definition was something he had only wholesale purchased from those revolutionary literary figures a few nights ago. Now he wanted to retail a little of it to her.

"Ha, ha, ha! That's a little more advanced than before. But..."

He thought, this is really unexpected. "Literature and art are a reflection of society," is there a more fashionable definition than that? He felt a little unconvinced. He made up his mind to ask her.

"Then, is there a more fashionable definition?"

He asked her, pretending to be calm and smiling.

"Hee, hee, hee... Mr. Lin..."

This time, he concentrated and focused, wanting to seriously absorb some knowledge from this Mrs. Tsuruko.

"...What kind of tea is this? It's so fragrant and lovely!"

"How unreasonable!"

After cursing under his breath, he replied to her with three words, very unhappily, "Tieguanyin."

"What a beautiful name, so artistic, hee, hee, hee."

"What you just said about the definition of literature and art, what should it be like to be considered the most fashionable?"

"You're still thinking about that? Forget it, Mr. Lin. I don't understand it very well either. I saw it in a very ordinary Japanese magazine, *Fujin Kōron*. The definition of literature given by leftist writers is, 'the voice of labor,' you know."

"Isn't that just a type of social reflection?"

"That's not right, Mr. Lin. Although it is a reflection of society, reactionary literature should be excluded, you know. This is the most cutting-edge definition of literature. But I don't agree with such a narrow definition. Perhaps we haven't grasped Ideologie yet."

Haiquan thought, right, right. Ideologie! This is the term that Mr. Chen Huamin often mentioned when lecturing him on literary theory that night, and he didn't quite understand it yet. How does Mrs. Tsuruko also know about these things? He was stunned and didn't reply for a while.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Discussions

Insisting on Being Seen Favorably

— Bian

Yesterday, Mr. "Wu" discussed being seen favorably at Peking University, and his meaning was not yet exhausted. I will add to his explanation: the Japanese have not yet attacked Peiping and Tianjin, but the universities of Peiping are needlessly alarmed, with incidents such as fleeing the examinations and advancing the holidays. This kind of phenomenon is indeed inappropriate. It not only shows the cowardly mentality of our people and the authorities, making the enemy even more arrogant in their advance, but on the other hand, with the highest institutions of learning displaying such phenomena, people become even more shaken, and social order can hardly be maintained. Peiping universities should be seen favorably and should even more be seen favorably.

But recently, looking at the telegrams in the newspaper, the day before yesterday there was:

"The Palace Museum Antiquities Are Packed and Ready to Be Transported South; Various Groups Still Decide to Oppose It."

Yesterday's telegram had:

"The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Telegraphed that the Archives Preservation Office Will Transport Important Files to Luoyang for Preservation."

This being the case, I cannot help but feel confused. On the one hand, the authorities do not allow students to flee the exams, do not allow the school authorities to advance the holidays, but on the other hand, they are packing up antiquities and archives to be transported south. It is true that antiquities and archives are quite important, and it is appropriate to transport them south as a precautionary measure to prevent unforeseen events. Is the life and property of students not worth half a cent? Assuming that they want to calm things down, how can they calm others if they themselves are not calm? Is this not an absolute contradiction?

I think that in any matter, there must first be a consistent approach. As the saying goes, "Without oneself being right, one cannot criticize others," and "Governing is not about many words, but about how vigorously one acts." Now, the national crisis is at hand. Rumors about Tianjin and Peiping will inevitably arise like bees. The government should first have a method to stabilize the overall situation and a plan to resist the enemy. This is the proper way to prevent people from being shaken. If there is no plan to resist the enemy, and yet one wants to force the general public to remain calm, that is already difficult to do. Moreover, how can one blame others for not being calm when one cannot be calm oneself?

Therefore, some sarcastic people say that the authorities only value antiquities and do not value the people. Although this statement is too harsh, judging from the facts, the origin of this statement may not be without reason.

Science

Changes in Vegetables and Rice

— Lin Xia

Calling for vegetables and eating rice, who wouldn't know how! One interruption leads to death. What exactly happens to the fragrant and fresh vegetables and rice that are eaten? What is excreted is yellow and smelly feces and urine. Perhaps many of the readers of this journal do not understand the changes in vegetables and rice that occur in their own bodies at all times!

The types of vegetables and rice we eat are extremely numerous. But in terms of the nutrients they contain, there are only three categories...

The first category... carbohydrates... are various foods containing starch and sugar, such as rice, wheat, and yams.

The second category... proteins... are foods such as egg white, tofu, and meat.

The third category... fats... are foods such as various oils and fats.

Although these three types of things are contained in various vegetables and rice to varying degrees, unless they are ground and dissolved in water, becoming a liquid that can penetrate the inner surface of blood vessels, they cannot be used by our bodies!

Therefore, vegetables and rice must undergo five changes...

First... they must be bitten and ground by the teeth;

Second... the saliva in the mouth must ferment the carbohydrates in the vegetables and rice, turning them into a permeable sugar solution;

Third... when swallowed, the gastric juice in the stomach turns the proteins in the vegetables and rice into a type of peptone;

Fourth... in the intestines, the bile secreted from the gallbladder first turns the fats and oils in the vegetables and rice into permeable emulsified fats.

Fifth... the pancreatic juice (also called pancreas, Shanghai people call it "jia gan") secreted from the pancreas further transforms the three nutrients in the vegetables and rice that have not been completely changed into sugar solution, peptone, and emulsified fat!

The transformed sugar solution, peptone, and emulsified fat then penetrate the mucous membranes of the mouth, stomach, and intestines, entering the blood vessels and circulating throughout the body. Further, two changes occur...

㈠ The oxygen inhaled in the lungs is attached to the blood cells and spread throughout the body.

Page 22

The oxygen reacts, producing heat and energy. The heat keeps our bodies warm! The energy allows our entire bodies to move.

㈡ In various parts of the body, it becomes new cells of muscle, skin, bone, blood, and brain, so our bodies can grow and maintain their original state.

When we are full, our bodies are warm! When we are sick and eat less, our entire bodies quickly become weak, this is the reason.

All of the above changes cannot be separated from water. Without water, no changes can occur. Therefore, everyone must drink a large amount of water every day. Being thirsty for a long time can also kill people.

Because the vegetables and rice we eat are not purely composed of carbohydrates, proteins, and fats, the three nutrients that are not completely changed, and other impurities, accumulate in the large intestine. However, roundworms and other bacteria that are not very harmful to humans feel that they are the ultimate delicacy! Thus, they develop and grow in the human large intestine, fermenting and decomposing them, producing several malodorous gases such as ammonia and hydrogen sulfide. When released alone, they become farts; when discharged with feces, they create the characteristic odor of feces.

Communication from Shop Employees

Dying for Face, Suffering While Alive

Dear Editor... I am an only son, with no brothers or sisters, only one younger sister. When I was eighteen years old, my father abandoned his loving mother, wife, orphaned son, and weak daughter and passed away; at that time, I was still studying in the second year of old-style middle school. When my father was alive, he was also a small official, and his income was not bad. However, he was generous by nature, with a great sense of "never leaving a surplus." Therefore, the situation after his death was very bleak. In the year following my father's death, my grandmother, due to missing her beloved son, became ill with grief and anger, and also followed her beloved son to the underworld. In all the funeral matters, my mother refused to reduce them in the slightest because she wanted to maintain appearances. She arranged the expenses for the funeral on the one hand, and planned for the tuition fees for my sister and me on the other hand, and still had to maintain the seven daily necessities, making it extremely difficult. Seven years ago, I graduated from a certain middle school in this city and entered the State-run Gams Bureau as a mid-level employee. I had a monthly income of about one hundred yuan, and the position was very secure. Seeing that I could stand on my own feet in society, my mother handed over the entire family burden to me in the New Year of the following year. She handed me a stack of account books. After a detailed review, I learned that the debt was about more than one thousand eight hundred dollars. The reason for this was mostly because of maintaining face. Although I personally do not approve of this method, I also know that this is a common problem in society, so I am very understanding of my mother and only grateful to her for her hard work in supporting the family for many years, without any resentment. Then, the issue of my marriage was raised. According to my mother, she very much wanted to hold a grand wedding in our hometown. At that time, because the previous debts had not been cleared, I advocated that it had to be frugal. Fortunately, the parents of the other party were old friends and knew my situation, and forgave everything. It was held hastily in my place of work, costing less than seven hundred dollars. After that, I immediately began to be frugal and clear the debts; until recently, it finally came to an end. During these seven years, although everything was frugal, I was not stingy with my sister's tuition fees. I deeply know that this is the foundation of her future happiness. This summer, it is calculated that she can graduate from high school; her fiancé - the son of a wealthy family in our hometown - is also scheduled to marry this winter. So our problems started again! According to my mother, it is necessary to have a certain scale; so as to avoid my sister being bullied in the future, and at the same time not to lose our family's face. But this lightly "a certain scale" four words, it is calculated that it will not be done without two thousand dollars. When I thought about it myself, the past seven years have been busy with nothing but debts. Now, although the debts have been cleared, but the children are growing up, and the standard of living is getting higher and higher; if I rashly agree, these debts of more than two thousand yuan, I am afraid it will be enough for me to suffer for thirteen or fourteen years? How long is life, the time to make money, at most only twenty or thirty years. Thinking like this; I politely refused, advocating frugality, and all expenses should be limited to seven hundred dollars. Because this is the total amount of expenses for my wedding. I ask myself that I can always be worthy of others. Who knew that my old mother, on hearing this, became very angry. She said very sternly, "When your grandmother died, I was a widow, and your father had no savings, and I still arranged everything decently; our family's face has been maintained until now. Now you are a man with a job, and your income is above average, how can you bear to lose face?" I dared not answer at the time. But thinking about it now, it seems too bitter to borrow money to marry my sister, and it is not necessary in fact; because my future brother-in-law, he is very wealthy. Sacrificing my own happiness, only to get a smile from others, is also too foolish; but the mother's command is difficult to disobey, what to do? (To be continued) Xu Shugao respectfully submits

× × × ×

Editor's note... Chinese people are too focused on face and disregard the facts, so the contradictory life of "dying for face and suffering while alive" can be seen everywhere. From the above letter from Mr. Xu, we can also find two points that are not economically reasonable. ㈠ Mr. Xu's father's income was not bad; but the result was no savings. Although he was generous, this method of using it as soon as it was in hand is also inappropriate. As a result, his virtuous wife and beloved son suffered countless pain.

㈡ Mr. Xu's mother, in her mother-in-law's funeral, disregarded her strength and stubbornly fought for the occasion. Although she could "fully perform the duties of a son" and "fully perform filial piety" in the blessing meeting; this method of enduring pain and wanting to be good is ultimately inappropriate. So as a result, Mr. Xu suffered a long-term (seven years) of pain. Now she still wants her son to do this for the matter of marrying his sister, it can really be said to be stubbornly obsessed.

However, Mr. Xu's personal past does have three points that are worthy of our admiration.

㈠ After discovering that his mother, when she was in charge of the family, had built a debt platform of one thousand eight hundred dollars, he could forgive her difficulties; without any resentment. The way of a son, to this point can already be said to be blameless.

㈡ In the midst of extreme difficulty, he can continue to provide his sister's tuition fees, taking care of her lifelong happiness. The brother's obligation can also be considered fulfilled.

㈢ When he got married, he was able to break the environment and save as much as possible. Now, when marrying his sister, although it is very difficult, he is willing to take out the same amount of money that he spent when he got married to give to his sister. It can also be considered generous.

We advise Mr. Xu to resolutely follow his own ideas, this is not wrong. In front of the old mother, he should gently explain when she is happy. The heart of loving a child is shared by everyone, and understanding is not difficult to imagine.

If you make a cocoon for yourself, then the most precious middle age of life will be ruined; and maybe you will end up like your father, leaving endless pain to your wife and children!

We also advise Mr. Xu's mother to finally repent for her past mistakes, which have already made her son very embarrassed; do not continue to be stubborn, making it impossible for her son to ever succeed.

Mr. Xu's sister should also take into account her brother's difficulties and remember his seven years of educational grace. In front of her mother, try to persuade her. I think a woman who has received secondary education can certainly understand this; and this method is most likely to make her mother change her mind, because half of her reason for advocating extravagance is to maintain face, and half is still afraid that her daughter will be bullied in the future.

Finally, I must loudly appeal to Mr. Xu's brother-in-law and his parents, as well as the general public, to quickly change their views and implement the legacy of Mr. Zhu, "Marrying a wife requires seeking a virtuous woman, do not count on a rich dowry."

Fiction

A Scholarly Family (Continued 9)

— Wang Zhongxian

(5) Sending Big Red Invitations for a Death

Mrs. Xia did not necessarily have to rely on her husband to send living expenses in order to make a living, but suddenly stopping the money that she had been accustomed to receiving every month, she always felt somewhat resentful. She wrote a letter to blame Zhongnan, who did not even reply with an empty letter of excuse, and this anger was truly extraordinary! Her old illness relapsed, the "qi" stuck in her chest, and it did not go down for several days. She invited Chinese and Western doctors everywhere, took medicine and had injections, all to no avail; all that was seen was her eyes rolled upwards, with more white than black. In the first two days of the onset, she could still yell in pain like a pig being slaughtered, but later she became too weak to cry out, her breathing was like that of an athlete in a twenty-five-mile race reaching the finish line, her throat and mouth were blocked by a pile of phlegm that was neither up nor down!

Seeing that the situation was not right, Ali ordered Lao Hu to send three or four urgent telegrams to Zhongnan's post, and the reply telegram said, "Mrs. has passed away, please Big Master Bodong preside over the funeral affairs, expenses to be frugal." The person was not even dead yet, and he had already begun to calculate for the dead! If this reply telegram were to be seen by Mrs., it would be like a death warrant urging her to return to heaven. Lao Hu and Ali discussed hiding it.

Mrs. Xia knew that her illness was incurable and difficult to recover, so she called Maosheng and Ali to her bedside and said in a barely audible voice...

"Maosheng, I have raised him with all my heart. After I die, I'm afraid he will suffer in that woman's hands. Although Ali is a servant girl, I have always treated you as a daughter. I will simply recognize you as a daughter now, then Maosheng will be your brother, and you must take care of him differently in the future, don't let that woman bully him, and I will secretly protect you! You have served me for a while, these few pieces of jewelry are considered your reward."

As she spoke, she randomly grabbed a few pieces of jewelry from a jewelry box beside her pillow and gave them to Ali, who took them with tears in her eyes and comforted Mrs. After a while, Mrs. also ordered Maosheng to change his address in the future, calling Ali "Sister" and calling Secretary Sang "Brother-in-law."

After another three or five days, Mrs. Xia actually passed away peacefully! Big Master Bodong and Fourth Master Jici came forward to handle the funeral affairs. Xia's family has many descendants, and there were quite a few people wearing mourning clothes to send off the funeral. Regarding the issue of Maosheng's qualification to hold the mourning tablet, some people in the clan had raised objections. Later, Bodong explained, "Zhongnan has not formally established an heir. Although Maosheng is not biological, the second room has not denied or expressed any opinion, so it is not convenient for others to make decisions for him." Therefore, Maosheng still performed as the protagonist in mourning clothes. Because this issue had not been resolved, no obituary was issued after Mrs. Xia's death.

When the news of the death reached Zhongnan's post, Xia Second Master widely sent big red wedding invitations, choosing an auspicious day to feast guests. Sending big red invitations for a death, there is no such reason! Someone opened his wedding invitation and suddenly realized that the invitation read...

Respectfully select a certain day of the month to hold a temple visit ceremony for Ms. Ai Ruohua.

Respectfully request the presence of the entire family Xia Zhongnan and daughter Daiqiu bowing

This is an invitation for a concubine to be promoted to the main wife, which is also said in a dignified manner, but Xia Nan is from Jiangnan, and there is no Xia family ancestral hall in the post where he is an official. This temple visit ceremony can only be performed by facing the palace and kowtowing remotely like the emperor's era. Under Xia Zhongnan's name is also dragging an oil bottle miss, this is hinting that Ms. Ai Ruohua is also a "second-married head miss." The drafter of this invitation can be considered to have put in a lot of effort!

Ms. Ai Ruohua's fate is really bad! She made a set of magnificent wedding dresses, preparing to make a big splash on the auspicious day, but unfortunately, the happy event had not yet arrived, and disaster flew in from the outside! It turned out that the political situation in the province had changed at that time, and the head of the province had received the news earlier and had slipped into the concession, issuing a telegram of resignation. Zhongnan managed the province's finances, and it was difficult to get away without going through the handover procedures. He heard that the superior had fled in a big way and also wanted to run away, but unfortunately he received the news too late, and someone was monitoring his actions. If he rashly left the province, he would inevitably make a fool of himself on the spot and be detained, which would be too embarrassing! (To be continued)
